Important News

Recent News on Bandit Suppression in Hunan Province

Wei and Liu Exchange Messages of Mutual Understanding

Hankou Correspondence: Since Zhu De, Mao Zedong, Peng Dehuai, Huang Gonglue, and their respective troops joined forces and entered Hunan from Jiangxi, He Jian, the commander-in-chief of the Fourth Route Army, believed that Pingxiang and Liuyang were dangerous and difficult to annihilate, so he decided to shorten the front line and lure the bandits deeper. This caused rumors, and the survivors of the Changsha massacre, like frightened birds, fled in droves. In fact, Hunan Province already has the four divisions of Wei Suzhong, Luo Fan, Ying, Liu Jianxu, and Tao Guang, the two brigades of Chen Guangzhong and Chen Wo, and the troops from Hubei Province entering Hunan include the four divisions of Luo Lin, Gong Bingfan, Li Yunlong, and Qian Dajun. The troops from Jiangxi Province are also more than two divisions. In terms of air force, in addition to the four existing aircraft, the squadron leader of the Fifth Aviation Squadron, Tian Xi, led four more aircraft on the first of this month, two of which returned to Hankou and two remained in Hunan, for a total of six aircraft, and the armored train team Xiang E Hao, the military strength is now stronger than before. Although according to a telegram from the captain of the Xiang E Hao armored train team, Luo Xiancheng, Zhu, Mao, Peng, and others, divided into several routes from Dongshan, Yong'an City, and Datupo, are advancing towards Changsha, the large army is gathered, and the defenses of the provincial capital are solid and will definitely not succeed. As for the rumors that Wei Suzhong and Liu Jianxu have disagreements, making the situation in Hunan difficult, Wei and Liu both telegraphed yesterday to dispel the rumors, which is also sufficient to prove their inaccuracy. The two telegrams are recorded as follows:

Wei Suzhong's telegram to Director Hu Xiaoyan (Director of the Fourth Route Army Office in Hankou), transferred to the brothers Xiang Sanrun, Jingluo, and others in Hunan Province: I have received your telegram with respect. My brother and Hui (Liu Jianxu) are both under the unified command of the commander-in-chief, and we have shared hardships and hopes for a long time. Now that the great enemy is at hand, even the hatred of killing one's father should be abandoned, let alone that my brother and Hui have no grievances. The rumors are half due to the fabrications of reactionaries. These people are blinded by material desires and do not cherish the people. Changsha has also been clamorous recently, and it has been relieved immediately after the joint announcement. Brothers in Hankou, I hope that you will convey my sincere feelings to all parties, so that they can see that the will of the generals of the Fourth Route Army is very unified. Respectfully, your brother Wei Suzhong.

Liu Jianxu's telegram to Hu Xiaoyan and transferred to brothers Yu Xiangsan and Ling Daru: I have received your telegram with respect. My brother and all the officers and men have been close friends in adversity for decades, sharing life and death, and are firmly united. We are working together harmoniously with Li (Wei Suzhong), and there is no disagreement. The plans for this attack and defense have been decided after direct consultation. Extraneous unconcerned politicians and frustrated soldiers have fabricated rumors and sowed discord for no reason, which is extremely hateful. Rumors stop with the wise, so there is no need to dispel them. I am honored by your inquiry, I hope you will understand. Respectfully, your brother Liu Jianxu.

Hunan Authorities Investigate Rumors

Letter to the Chamber of Commerce Inquiring Whether Reactionaries are Spreading Rumors

The Chamber of Commerce Replies Requesting That the War Situation at the Front Be Announced in Summary

Changsha Correspondence: After the Fourth Route Army withdrew from Liucheng and lured the bandits deeper, the citizens of Changsha were in a panic, as if a great disaster was about to happen. Supporting the old and carrying the young, more than 50,000 people fled to Hankou and Gao. There were also rumors that the political situation was about to change. He Jian and Liu Jianxu heard that these rumors came from the Chamber of Commerce and sent a letter to inquire. The Chamber of Commerce replied immediately upon receiving the letter, stating that the Chamber had not heard of what was mentioned in the letter and that the family members of military personnel were moving, and armed soldiers were escorting luggage in a continuous stream, causing the people to panic. The Chamber of Commerce has always maintained calm, and its colleagues have not left their posts, and all stores are operating as usual. The various rumors are not responsible, etc. The exchange of letters between the two parties is disclosed below:

Headquarters' Letter to the Chamber of Commerce: The remaining bandits of Peng, Huang, Zhu, and Mao are still attempting a last-ditch struggle after their defeat. Our route army, in cooperation with friendly troops, is luring them out of the mountains in order to encircle and annihilate them. The military deployment is very secure, and the security of the provincial capital is not a concern. However, in recent days, the public's morale has been unusually turbulent, and it is no wonder that they are like frightened birds. Reactionaries, being insane, are trying to take advantage of this opportunity to fabricate all kinds of nonsensical rumors to disrupt the situation, which is extremely hateful. Yesterday afternoon, it was suddenly rumored that the political situation would change that night and that something would break out at a certain time. People were like frightened birds, passing the word around. When asked where they got it from, nine out of ten said that the news came from the Chamber of Commerce. Our department believed at the time that it was too worthless and could be proven that night, so we did not investigate it further. However, the mouths of the public not only affect security but also have a significant impact on your Chamber. How did the rumors originate, and are there any reactionaries in your Chamber spreading rumors? The responsible personnel of your Chamber should pay attention to this and maintain security.

Chamber of Commerce's Reply to the Headquarters: We respectfully reply that we have received your letter stating that rumors occurred yesterday and that we heard that they were spread by our Chamber, and we are asked to pay attention to them to maintain security, etc. Our Chamber's responsibility is to ensure the safety of the business community. If there are rumors, the business of merchants will be greatly affected. We would not even have time to close the doors, let alone want to spread rumors for no reason, causing mutual suspicion and harming ourselves. As for the rumors mentioned in your letter that the political situation would change yesterday, we not only do not believe it but also have not heard as much detail as stated in your letter. As for the so-called nine out of ten, who are they, and who is spreading this saying, which must be attributed to our Chamber? We sincerely do not know their intention. Even today, Chief of Staff Tang of the newly formed 22nd Division came to the Chamber and said that a pontoon bridge had been built at Nanhugang, and when asked of the Headquarters, it was said that it was at the request of our Chamber. However, our Chamber not only did not make this request but also did not send anyone to your department to make any suggestions. Even yesterday, the captain of the water police came to the Chamber and said that if merchants wanted to build a pontoon bridge, they had to make a formal written request, but our Chamber never made a decision. From this alone, it can be seen that the previous rumors did not originate from our Chamber. Furthermore, in recent days, the family members of military personnel have been moving, and armed soldiers have been escorting luggage in a continuous stream, causing the people to panic. Our Chamber has always maintained calm, and its colleagues have not left their posts, and all stores are still operating as usual. At this time, when the flames are high in front, the actions of the military are related to the observation and listening of the people. However, the military has suddenly moved to the rear, and the people do not know the truth, causing them to panic. We hope that you will announce the movement of the troops and the war situation at the front at any time in summary, so that you can calm the people's hearts and eliminate any rumors without any intervention. As for the question in your letter about whether there are reactionaries, merchants have no political minds or factions. This is what our Chamber can be confident in. The previous content of the letter is respectfully replied, and we hope that you will consider and implement it.

Tan Daoyuan's Division Returns to Jiangxi to Suppress Communists

Deputy Division Commander Yue Has Arrived in the Provincial Capital

Jiangxi Troops Enter Hunan to Pursue and Attack Communist Bandits

Nanchang Correspondence: Commander-in-Chief Lu and all sectors of the province believe that the land is full of bandits, and the bandit areas are vast, and the original troops are insufficient to be allocated, causing the people of various counties to be in dire straits and displaced. They have repeatedly telegraphed the Central Government and Commander-in-Chief Jiang, requesting that capable troops be sent to Jiangxi to assist in the suppression, in order to relieve the people from suffering. When Zhu Mao approached Nanxun, Jiang immediately telegraphed an order for one regiment of the 150th Brigade to return to Jiangxi first, and the rest to continue to set off. Now, the 149th Brigade of the division arrived in Jiujiang on the 28th of last month. Yue Sen, the deputy division commander and commander of the 149th Brigade, arrived in Xun from Beijing and took the Nanxun Road night train to the province at 12:00 p.m. on the 31st. When the train arrived at Niuhang Station, there were many welcomers. After Yue got off the train, he crossed the river and entered the city. This morning, Mr. Yue went to visit Commander-in-Chief Lu and Director Zhang's private residence to report on the past operations and ask for instructions on future bandit suppression plans. It is said that the brigade was ordered to station in the Tujiapu area of Nanxun Road to take care of the defenses of Jiujiang and northern Jiangxi. The two brigades of Cheng Guangyao and Luo Shouyi will also arrive successively. All sectors are preparing to hold a welcoming meeting because Tan's division has returned to Jiangxi. Once Director Tan arrives in the province, it can be held to express welcome.

On the 27th, a Central Army airplane dropped bombs in the sky over Beiping. One bomb fell near the residence of Wang Jingwei and damaged a corner of a certain family's house. This is a photo taken after the house was destroyed.

After the communist bandits Zhu, Mao, Peng, Huang, He, and Kong held a fake military conference in Wanzai, they divided into four routes to attack Changsha again. Zhu and Mao passed through the north of Liling from Wanzai, Peng and Huang passed through the Liuyang Avenue from Xiutong, and He Long and Kong also launched separately on the Hubei border. From the 25th to the 26th, the fighting in Liuyang was extremely fierce. According to news from the Ninth Route Army Headquarters, Director He has transferred the two divisions of Gong Bingfan and Luo Lin from Pingjiang to Changsha, and the troops of Tao Guang, Chen Guangzhong, and Dai Douyuan of the Fourth Route Army are guarding the area along Monkey Stone, Yuhuating, and Laodao River, with very tight defenses. After Commander-in-Chief Lu received the telegrams from He, he also ordered the vanguard brigade of Dai Yue of the 18th Division to advance from Xiutong across Pingliu, closely following Zhu Mao and Peng Huang. Yesterday, a telegram was received from Dai Yue, stating that Zhu Mao and Peng Huang are planning to disturb Hunan again, and the brigade is now transferring the heavy artillery battalion to Hunan to pursue and attack, encircling them from three sides in the hope of annihilating the bandits near Changsha.

In eastern Jiangxi, Commander-in-Chief Lu ordered Zhang's regiment in Yujiang to stop suppressing the communist bandits in Poyang. On the 28th, it joined forces with the warship Minzu and the machine gun company of the 18th Division to recapture the county. Zhang's regiment is currently cooperating with County Magistrate Jiang to pursue the remaining bandits. At the same time, the Zhejiang provincial government has also appointed a large team to advance from Changshan and station in Yushan and Shangrao, attacking the bandits from behind in the hope of annihilating them.

Regarding the security of the provincial capital, Lu Dipin built fortifications near Nanchang in June in order to consolidate the provincial capital. The Nanchang General Chamber of Commerce raised 30,000 yuan for construction costs. A new type of trench and electric fence were built around the city. Later, when Changsha fell and Zhu Mao approached Nanxun, Lu became more vigilant and raised funds from the provincial government to build another layer of fortifications. Now, in addition to these two layers of fortifications, another layer of obstacles has been built. The three layers of fortifications have been completed recently and are very solid. In addition to the commander of the 18th division, Zhang, the chief of staff of the Ninth Route Army, Xiao, and the brigade commander of the 53rd brigade, Wang, who inspected them by flying around, Lu also inspected the fortifications around the city on the morning of August 27th at about 9:00 a.m., accompanied by Chief of Staff Xie, on the Moshi warplane. The plane hovered in the air for about thirty minutes before landing. It is said that Lu is very satisfied with these fortifications. After this, only a thousand soldiers will be able to defend against the communist bandits, and the 10,000 people of Nanchang City can rest assured.

Ji'an Cracks Down on the Communist Party's General Headquarters

Dozens of Important Communist Bandits Arrested

Nanchang Correspondence: Ji'an is the center of culture, commerce, and transportation in western Jiangxi, and also the throat of transportation between Ganzhou and the provincial capital. Its position is extremely important. Since Zhu Mao established Ninggang and Yongxin in western Jiangxi as their base in the 16th year of the Republic [1927], they have long desired Ji'an and have been unwilling to give up. This time, when Zhu Mao fled east, they still left bandit troops, the pseudo-20th Army and the 22nd Army, to surround Ji'an, attempting to succeed at any cost. On July 1st, Duan Qifeng, the army commander of the pseudo-20th Army, led more than 10,000 bandits to attack Ji'an several times with great ferocity. However, because the important areas around the city and along the river were fortified with electric fences, trenches, bunkers, and artillery forts, and there were also the "National People's Rights" and "People's Rights" warships patrolling the river, preventing the bandits from crossing, Ji'an was finally spared. Now, according to Ji'an's wireless report on the 27th, after the communist bandits repeatedly attacked the city and suffered disastrous defeats, they realized that armed force would be difficult to succeed with. Therefore, they changed their strategy and secretly sent assassination squad leader Chen Cherui, arson squad leader Zeng Guotang, and movement squad leader Huang Hansheng to infiltrate Ji'an to organize institutions and conduct secret activities, hoping to coordinate from within and without. Fortunately, the military police's inspection was effective, and the communist party's general headquarters in Ji'an was cracked down. Chen, Zeng, Huang, and dozens of important members were arrested, and many documents, plans, and reactionary propaganda materials were confiscated. The New 13th Division's military court is currently handling the case strictly.

Furthermore, Gujiang is the necessary route from Ji'an to Anfu, and was previously occupied by communist bandits. Anfu was also captured by bandits. Now, after Deng's division defeated the communist bandits, Anfu was recovered. The county magistrate has already returned to the county to handle the aftermath. (August 28th)

Fuzhou on High Alert

Fuzhou Correspondence: After the end of the second phase of the war in Fujian Province, the local area gradually began to lift martial law. Now, the provincial government believes that the third phase of the war is about to begin. Chen Guohui's brigade and Lin Qinglong's regiment of the Fujian Southern Provincial Defense Army's First Division have already advanced from Yongchun to Dehua and Zhangtian. Liu Zongyi's unit of the Fujian Eastern Provincial Police Force and Lin Bingzhou's regiment of the naval and land joint teams have already advanced from Shouning to Zhenghe and Songxi. Liu Heding's division in Fuzhou has also completed its deployment, and will soon be able to cooperate with Liang Jichuan and Huang Bingwu's units in Yongtai and Xixiang to advance towards Gutian and Minqing, taking a three-sided encirclement of Lu's troops. Compared with the first and second phases of the war, where only Fuzhou fought alone, the scope is even wider. The provincial capital is an important rear defense base, and its importance is extremely high. Yesterday afternoon, Yang Shuzhuang specially convened a meeting with Liu Shangzhi, the Fuzhou martial law commander, Mao Zhencai, the Minhou Fortress commander, Guo Yongrong, the Public Security Bureau chief, and Shen Ke, the Water Public Security Bureau chief, and decided to announce special martial law on land and water from today onwards. Regarding the water aspects, all ships entering from various ports must be strictly inspected by the Minhou Fortress Command before being allowed to disembark passengers and unload goods. Ships traveling to and from the inner harbor of the Min River will have inspection stations set up by the Water Public Security Bureau at Xigang Hongshan Bridge and Nangang Sanbao Road. All passing ships can only be released after inspection. On the land aspect, the martial law command will work with the city's Public Security Bureau to send armed soldiers and police to inspect pedestrians at important locations in the city. Those who carry firearms and ammunition privately without a permit will be dealt with by military law. At the same time, military police detective teams and inspection teams will conduct spot checks on suspicious households to see if they are privately hiding military supplies. The Lianjia system for each shop, which had been suspended since the lifting of local martial law, will now be reinstated by the city's Public Security Bureau, which will issue 24 articles of the Lianjia method to each shop to be implemented again. The provincial government's gatekeeping has also been especially tightened since yesterday. Additional guards have been assigned to all locations within the government and around its perimeter. Those not wearing the government's emblem will absolutely not be allowed to enter, and even those wearing the emblem must have their belongings opened for inspection. Yang Shuzhuang stays in the provincial government day and night and does not return home. The aircraft, which had been suspended for a long time, were also redeployed yesterday, with two planes dispatched to the northwestern front line to scout the enemy's situation. In recent days, the 56th Division and the Marine Corps have been test-firing artillery and torpedoes in the Kangshan and Jinjishan areas of Dongmen, and the rumbling sounds have shaken people's eardrums. The current situation in Fuzhou is gradually becoming tense again. (August 30th)

Hubei Special Commissioner's Office Holds Tax Revenue Rectification Meeting

Hankou Correspondence: Since Li Jihong took office as the Special Commissioner of Finance for the North, in view of the sluggish tax revenue in the province and the difficulty in coping, he urgently considered ways to rectify it. This afternoon (1st) at 3:00 PM, he specially convened the heads of various national tax agencies in the province to hold a meeting to reorganize tax revenue. The representatives present included Li Muqing, Director of the Special Tax Office; Luo Ting, Director of the Stamp Tax Bureau; Xie Fencheng, Director of the Cigarette Tax Bureau; Zhang Zimei, Director of the Tobacco and Alcohol Affairs Bureau; Chen Yongqing, Director of the Salt Transport Bureau; Zeng Luda, Director of the Flour Tax Bureau; Tu Zhenhu, Director of the Parcel Post Tax Bureau; Liang Rongsun, Supervisor of the Wuchang Customs; Xi Debing, Supervisor of the Jianghan Customs; Wang Changquan, Director of the Salt Affairs Audit Office; and Wan Yukun, Supervisor of the Xindi Customs, and more than ten others. Li Jihong, as chairman, first gave an opening speech, roughly stating that Hubei Province is located in the center of the country and its commerce is prosperous. In the past, national taxes were known as a surplus area. However, recently, due to the anti-rebellion military campaign and the disturbances of the communist bandits, tax revenue has been declining day by day. Since I was ordered to come to Hubei to preside over tax affairs, I am ashamed of my mediocrity and inability to assume such an important task. However, considering that at this time, when military salaries are huge and government expenses are pressing, since I have accepted the heavy trust of Minister Song, I should try to take on the heavy difficulties and strive to rectify and adjust. I hope that all of you present will take the friendship of fellow passengers and thoroughly discuss this matter to help us get through this difficult time. Next, the attendees took turns to reply, and repeatedly stated the current situation of sluggish tax revenue and the difficulties in handling affairs. Then, they discussed Li's proposal for reorganizing tax revenue. The original proposal roughly stated: After investigating, Hubei Province is located in the center of the country, and Hankou's commerce has always been known to be prosperous. National tax revenue should be more prosperous than other provinces. Since the anti-rebellion military campaign, the communist bandits have caused disturbances in the rear, traffic has been blocked, and commercial transport has been hindered, resulting in a decrease in revenue. All agencies feel the difficulties. However, the Hubei branch treasury should pay 2.51 million yuan for military expenses every month, and about 100,000 yuan for Wuhan University, the Army Survey Bureau, and other government expenses, all of which are fixed amounts and must be disbursed on a monthly basis. My office is responsible for disbursing and remitting national treasury funds, auditing accounts, and planning and reorganizing methods. I, Hongji, was ordered to take over this position. Since the beginning of my appointment, after reviewing the files, I learned that as of now, more than 900,000 yuan is owed in military expenses and more than 100,000 yuan is owed in university expenses. The reason for this is that tax revenue is insufficient for disbursement. At this time, when military salaries are huge and great attention is paid to political training, military, academic, and government expenses cannot be reduced. The only way is to actively reorganize tax revenue. Jihong and the heads of various agencies will take the friendship of fellow passengers and thoroughly study this matter to get through this difficult time, so as to avoid delays. I would like to state my thoughts below: (1) The salaries are to be issued urgently. I would like to ask each agency to estimate the actual revenue in the most recent three months in order to cope with the situation. The Hubei treasury should disburse a total of more than 2.6 million yuan for military and government expenses every month, and military expenses are issued in six installments of more than 400,000 yuan every five days. The amount is huge and the time is urgent, and cannot be delayed. Recently, due to the shortage of funds remitted by various agencies, the arrears have been very large. Jihong was ordered to succeed and was personally instructed by the minister to first raise funds on time and then clear the arrears. I should try to comply with this, but my office does not directly receive funds, and it is impossible to cope with the situation without the joint efforts of all national tax agencies to seek relief. I would like to ask each agency to accurately estimate the actual and reliable revenue in the most recent three months and submit a monthly list to my office so that it can be submitted to the ministry as a confirmed revenue to be used for salaries. (2) Establish an accurate comparison table of tax revenue for national tax agencies in Hubei Province. Previously, the national tax agencies in Hubei Province had a fixed revenue amount. However, in recent years, due to changes in tax rates or changes in collection methods, it has been difficult to implement according to the original comparison in practice. It is difficult to reconcile and assess. I would like to ask each agency to refer to the actual revenue in the 17th, 18th, and 19th years of the Republic [1928, 1929, 1930], combined with the current collection status and local conditions, to separately determine the peak and off-season periods and create an accurate comparison table for reference. This table will be submitted to the ministry for approval and implementation. (3) Each agency should submit a reorganization plan for the tax revenue under its jurisdiction to the ministry for approval. Although Hubei Province's production is not rich, its shipping routes and transportation are convenient, and merchants are densely packed. Since trade is flourishing, tax revenue is increasing day by day. Those who preside over the monopoly administration should first eliminate accumulated malpractices, and then observe the situation, open up tax sources, and increase tax revenue. At this time, when military expenses are huge, this is especially important. However, how to reorganize should be determined by each competent authority based on the current tax situation, and a practical reorganization plan should be prepared and submitted to the ministry for approval and implemented step by step. (4) Each agency's revenue should still be deposited in full in the Central Bank of China on a daily basis in accordance with the ministry's order. Last year, each agency's revenue was instructed by the minister to be deposited in the Central Bank of China. Those who violate this will be treated as fraudulent. The former special commissioner Chen has already sent letters to each agency to follow this procedure. Currently, it is found that the number of deposit accounts in the Central Bank of China for each agency is still small, or some agencies have not deposited all funds on a daily basis. I would like to ask each agency to deposit all tax funds collected in the future in the Central Bank of China on a daily basis in order to comply with the ministry's order and facilitate transfer and reporting. (5) Each agency's daily cash receipts and disbursements statements and daily revenue reports should be sent to my office on a daily basis starting from September 1st for transfer and reporting. The daily cash receipts and disbursements and daily revenue reports of each agency were originally required to be submitted on a daily basis. Currently, many agencies have not been able to follow this procedure, or have submitted them in batches every few days. It is difficult for my office to reconcile and transfer the reports. I would like to ask that starting from September 1st, the original regulations should still be followed and submitted to my office on a daily basis for transfer and reporting. All of the above points were discussed and approved by all attendees. Next, the method of adjusting tax revenue for the next three months was discussed. The salt tax and special tax are the most important sources of tax revenue in Hubei Province. However, the salt tax revenue will be gradually used to repay loans in September, October, and November. Only the Yisha area can collect 250,000 yuan in November. Therefore, we must pay attention to the special tax. Li Muqing, Director of the Special Tax Office, agreed to pay 1 million yuan per month. Li Jihong requested an additional loan of 500,000 yuan to meet urgent needs, limited to three months. Other tax revenue agencies must also strengthen rectification in order to increase revenue. All representatives also agreed. The meeting did not adjourn until 5:00 PM. (August 1st)

Wuhu Merchants Oppose Relocation of Rice Market

Wuhu Correspondence: Anhui Province is known throughout the country for its rice production, and the Wuhu rice market also occupies an important position in domestic commerce. The prosperity or decline of various industries in Wuhu depends on the rice market, and the increase or decrease in Anhui Province's tax revenue also depends on the prosperity or decline of the rice market. Therefore, the Wuhu rice market is no less than the economic center of Anhui Province. In recent years, although the rice market has gradually declined, the depressed market is still maintained. The provincial capital suddenly had a rice market preparation office, intending to move the Wuhu rice market to the capital. People in Anhui had appealed to the government due to the relationship of interests. Unexpectedly, the capital's rice market preparation office has recently been approved and filed. Various industries in Wuhu were greatly panicked by this news. This afternoon at 2:00 PM, various business associations held an emergency meeting at the General Chamber of Commerce and resolved to telegraph the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance and Industry to request the cancellation of this proposal in order to protect the lifeline of Wuhu. The text of the telegram is recorded as follows: (Nanjing respectfully submitted to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Industry) Anhui Province's commerce is centered on the Wuhu rice market. Recently, it was heard that the capital is establishing a rice market preparation office. The news has spread and everyone is panicked and at a loss. Anhui Province is a rice-producing area, and the rice market has been concentrated in Wuhu for a long time. Rice from various counties in southern Anhui is transported to Wuhu by small boats from inland river ports. There is less risk of wind and waves, and it can be sold nearby. If the rice market is moved to the capital, it will have to travel far across the Yangtze River. Who will bear the responsibility for the risks? If we must change the rules, the rice donation will be cut off, there will be no money for education, and scholars will be in trouble. Anhui farmers have limited harvests. A small amount of transportation can be sold for value. Now we are abandoning the near and seeking the far, and the farmers will be in trouble. There are more than 10,000 boatmen, total packaging, and porter workers, and their livelihoods will be cut off. Workers will be in trouble. Merchants in various industries have no rice to transfer, and various businesses will inevitably decline sharply. Merchants will be in trouble. If this policy is implemented, it will not only make the four classes of people in Wuhu suffer, but also harm all counties in Anhui Province. Our Anhui belongs to the central government's protection. How can we bear to see the commercial port become a ruin and not pay attention to it? Moreover, this year's rice famine has resulted in a loss of more than 80,000 yuan for flat rice sales. We have requested the provincial government to compensate with two points of the rice donation. Who will compensate for the loss caused by the relocation of the rice market? At today's meeting, the various business associations were filled with indignation, and they all said that moving the rice market is tantamount to making all merchants unemployed. Therefore, we have described the beginning and end of the matter in detail and urgently implore your office to review and verify it and issue an order to abolish the capital's rice market preparation office in order to preserve the lives of the four classes of people in Anhui. We are eagerly awaiting orders. (August 1st)

National News 2

Jiangsu Province Organizes Guard District

The Jiangsu Provincial Government Committee previously resolved to establish a provincial capital guard district in the six counties of Zhenjiang, Jurong, Danyang, Yangzhou, Jiangdu, and Yizheng. The organization charter and organization methods are recorded as follows:

Organization Charter (1) This guard district is organized by the Provincial Government Committee. (2) The guard area is temporarily designated as the jurisdiction of the six counties of Zhenjiang, Jurong, Danyang, Yangzhou, Jiangdu, and Yizheng. (3) The guard district shall have one district chief to handle the matters of clearing bandits and communists in the entire district, and one director to assist the district chief in performing his duties. (4) The chief of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau and the county magistrates of each county shall be responsible for handling the affairs of clearing bandits and communists in their respective jurisdictions under the direction of the district chief. (5) The guard district shall establish the following sections to handle various matters in the district: (1) General Affairs Section, (2) Military Law Section, (3) Propaganda Section. (6) Each bureau and county shall establish a guard committee, and its members shall be composed of six to eight local fair people selected and appointed by each bureau and county. The chairman of the committee shall be the chief of each bureau and county. (7) The guard district shall gather a number of bandit suppression troops and establish a bandit suppression commander who shall be responsible for clearing bandits and communists under the command of the district chief. (8) Each bureau and county shall select and compile a number of police teams and defense regiments from the existing ones for guerrilla warfare. (9) The detailed rules for handling affairs in each bureau and county shall be determined separately. (10) The guard period is temporarily set at three months to be completed, but it may be extended by submitting a request to the provincial government based on the circumstances. (11) The chiefs of each bureau and county shall be granted the title of military judge by the Commander-in-Chief's Office upon the recommendation of the Commander of the Bandit Suppression Force for the entire province. (12) The guard expenses shall be budgeted by the district chief and submitted to the provincial government for approval.

Organization Methods (1) The district shall have one district chief who shall be concurrently the Commander of the Bandit Suppression Force for the entire province of Jiangsu. (2) The district shall have one director who shall be concurrently the Chief of the Third Section of the Department of Civil Affairs. (3) The district shall establish the following sections: (1) General Affairs Section, with one section chief and a number of section members, to manage command, dispatch, and matters not belonging to other sections. (2) Military Law Section, with one section chief and a number of section members, to manage the interrogation of bandits and communists and the investigation of various matters. (3) Propaganda Section, with one section chief and a number of section members, to manage propaganda matters. (4) The personnel for handling affairs in each section of the district shall be concurrently appointed by the district chief from the personnel handling affairs in the Security Department of the Department of Civil Affairs. Personnel may be selected and appointed when necessary. (5) The district shall have one bandit suppression commander who shall be concurrently the regiment commander of the 4th Security Regiment. (6) The bandit suppression troops in the district, in addition to the Security Regiment, shall be selected and compiled from the existing police teams and county defense regiments of the 5th Water District and each county and the Public Security Bureau of the provincial capital. (7) When it is necessary to discuss the strategy of bandit suppression in the seven districts, the district chief shall convene a meeting to decide. (8) The application expenses for the district shall be reported separately by the Security Department. (9) The detailed rules for handling guard affairs in each county and the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau shall be formulated by the county magistrates of each county and the chief of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau with reference to the organization charter and this organization method, but must be reported to the district headquarters for record. (10) The district shall not separately print official seals. All documents and orders shall use the official seal of the Security Department. (11) If there are any matters not covered by these methods, they may be amended at any time and submitted to the provincial government for record.

Communist Bandits on Zhejiang Border Will Be Eliminated Soon

During the incident on the Zhejiang-Jiangxi border, the Fujian bandit He Jinbiao and others colluded with the communist bandits in Wenzhou, hoping to disturb the Zhejiang border. The original defense troops there were few in number. In order to lure the enemy in, they retreated on purpose in order to annihilate them in one fell swoop. Although Taishun was once captured, the provincial government ordered the dispatch of the 5th and 6th Security Regiments and two water police patrol ships to assist in the suppression together with the 4th Regiment stationed in Yongjia. The communist bandits were unable to support themselves and fled in droves. Yesterday, the provincial government received a telegram from Regiment Commander Gan of the 4th Regiment reporting that the 1st, 12th, and part of the 9th companies of the regiment had recovered Taicheng on the 30th, and local order had been completely restored. As for Jinyun, the local garrison was only two platoons of the Security Team because the communist bandits took advantage of the vacancy to disturb the area. They temporarily retreated to Yongkang. Later, the provincial government ordered the dispatch of Zhao Ying of the 7th Regiment to suppress them. The communist bandits were shocked and fled upon hearing the news and withdrew from the city. It is expected that after the troops of the 7th Regiment arrive, they can be completely eliminated. As for the Jiangxi border, since the recovery of Yushan, the defense has become more consolidated. The provincial government has telegraphed the troops entering Jiangxi to stop advancing and properly defend.

Hat and Shoe Industry Resolves to Raise Prices: There are a total of four or fifty hat and shoe stores in the city. Shuangxi Shipping Boat Robbed Midway: Recently, robberies have occurred frequently in the rural areas of our county, and the villagers are restless. Regarding the burning of tax receipts: Gu Li-peng and others of Xuanling Township protested against grain levies due to disaster-related cases, climbed and destroyed the Han Er drawing and Cao Guo's house, and burned the tax receipts from the 17th and 18th years. The County Finance Bureau has presented this matter to the government, stating that the case involves criminal offenses. In addition to submitting the case file to the County Court for legal punishment, instructions have been requested from the Finance Department to instruct the Finance Bureau to deliberate and review the method of supplementary levy for the burnt grain receipts from the 17th and 18th years in order to emphasize grain taxation.

Zhenjiang

The Chang Le Township Militia Corps Robbed: The Chang Le Township Peng Dun Militia Corps in Zhenjiang, equipped with six new rifles to defend against bandits, was suddenly attacked by numerous bandits the other night. They swarmed the corps, surrounded it on all sides, and completely seized their firearms. The head of the militia corps, Kang Qiyue, resisted them and was beaten by the bandits. He has now reported this to the head of the village corps, requesting that the authorities be notified and that the bandits be apprehended and brought to justice.

People from Xinzhou Come to the Provincial Capital to Petition: There have been frequent collapses in Xinzhou, Jiangbei. Recently, cracks have appeared in the land, causing unrest among the local residents. Yesterday, they gathered a crowd and sent representatives, including a Mr. Wang, to the provincial capital. Several hundred people pleaded with the provincial government and requested subsidies and appropriate measures to ensure their safety.

Regimental Commander Huang From Qingjiang Comes to the Provincial Capital: Huang Meixing, the regimental commander of the 266th Regiment of the 133rd Brigade stationed in Qingjiang, arrived in the provincial capital by boat on the 2nd. He reported to the provincial government and the security department on the disturbances caused by the bandits in Yanghe, Suqian, and the search and suppression efforts. He also reported the beginning and end of the fall of Yugou Town in Qingjiang, the reasons for failing to send troops to rescue, and inquired about the request for the 1st Regiment of the Xuhuai Sea Guerrilla Force to be stationed in Qingjiang. He has not yet received any telegrams from the headquarters or the provincial government, so he is seeking instructions. It is reported that Huang came to the provincial capital because the 5th Company of his regiment was accused of investigating Xiao Mingqin, the principal of Suqian Middle School in Huaiyin, and he reported the details of this case to the security department.

The Garrison Headquarters Arrests Important Criminals: The Capital Garrison Headquarters previously sent personnel to Zhenjiang to jointly arrest eight important criminals, including a Mr. Jiang, with the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau. After briefly interrogating them in Zhenjiang, they were escorted to the capital on the morning of the 2nd.

Changshu

Ransom Nearly Leads to a Huge Swindle: Su Liangqing's family in Shazhou City, Changyinsha, Changshu County, was robbed last mid-month. Su's wife, children, and a private tutor were kidnapped, totaling eight people. The bandits demanded a ransom of 150,000 yuan. Su initially ignored this due to the exorbitant ransom. However, he soon received another letter from the bandits, suddenly reducing the ransom from 150,000 yuan to 25,000 yuan, and arranging a meeting at a certain inn. Su believed that a negotiation was possible at this time and personally went to the agreed location. However, he was unable to make contact and posted an implied message on the message board. After waiting for two days, no one showed up, so he returned with the money. Only later did he learn that the letter was a forgery by a swindler. Fortunately, Su was not fooled, but the whereabouts of the kidnapped people remain unknown. Yesterday, a hostage who escaped from a bandit den in Da'an Port reported that the Su family hostages are still being held in the bandit den, but in a separate room with only one entrance. Two bandits take turns guarding day and night. Su's wife, children, and the tutor have their faces covered with towels during the day and their feet tightly bound at night, tied together so they cannot move. The children often cry out in pain, and the bandits silence them by burning their arms with lit cigarettes. Upon hearing this news, the Su family is extremely worried and plans to send someone to negotiate. However, the bandits are still demanding a ransom of 150,000 yuan for the release of all the hostages.

Mingguang

Execution of Bandits by Firing Squad: The 7th Regiment of the 2nd Cavalry Division stationed in Mingguang previously approved the self-defense corps to send Zhu Debiao (aka Zhu Lao Jiu), a notorious bandit from Dingyuan. After interrogation by Regimental Commander Wang and submission to the division commander for review, the death penalty was approved. The bandit was executed by firing squad at the execution ground outside the North Gate yesterday.

The Chen Xuefeng Family Kidnapped: More than thirty bandits, armed with weapons, suddenly broke into Chen Xuefeng's house in Hongxinji at around 7 AM yesterday (the 28th), firing shots to intimidate. Chen's grandson, Tongxin, was wounded, and seven members of the family were kidnapped.

Rugao

Bandits Set Fire to Tea Hermitage: The Rulai Temple in Cha'antou (Tea Hermitage) near Rugao County (over ten li from the city), was suddenly attacked by dozens of bandits at around 1 AM on the 29th. They set fire to the temple, causing a blaze that lit up the sky. They also fired two shots to prevent people from rescuing the temple. The temple was burned down, including three rooms in the east wing, two rooms in the west wing, and two side rooms. All the objects inside the temple were burned. The monks of the temple were forced to remain silent under threat of being shot.

Militia Suppresses Bandits in the Western Countryside: The people of Meichengzhuang in the western countryside are practicing self-defense by organizing militia to defend against bandits. As previously reported, the militia, together with the stationed troops, searched and suppressed a bandit den in Gujiaxiang the other day, killing fifty bandits on the spot and destroying many bandit strongholds.

Nantong

Expanding and Building Ring Roads: The city base in Tongyi is undergoing a division of land and foundation grading after the Education Bureau cleared and demarcated the ring road lines. This work is currently underway.

Provincial Government Explains Bandit Suppression by Military Law: The county government previously received an order from the province to punish captured bandits by military law. Because it is not currently handling judicial affairs, it specially submitted a request to the province for instructions. A telegram was received on the 2nd, stating that military law refers to military law organs. In the future, captured bandits should be sent to the Provincial Bandit Suppression Command or the Songhu Garrison Command nearby for interrogation and punishment.

Naval Marines Land to Guard Tong City: After the military and police opened fire on the bandits in Pingchao, the defenses of the city were requested by all sectors to have the Hai Rui and Ying Rui ships of the stationed Tonghai Navy send marines to land and be responsible for guarding. The headquarters was set up in the clubhouse.

The Remaining Bandits in Pingchao Reassemble: The bandits at the border between Tongzhou and Rugao burned and looted Wu Jiao Qiao town, then entrenched themselves in Siyu Port. After the military and police in Pingchao advanced to suppress them, many were killed or captured, and the main force collapsed. At 8 PM on the 1st night, they reassembled in the area, claiming that they would return the firearms collected at the end of the month and leave. The provincial and county police intercepted them. By noon on the 2nd, the bandits fled to Zhen Tao. The disaster in Xin Dingjiamiao and other areas is quite severe.

Limiting Advance Payments for Wounded Soldiers' Supplies: The 31st Rear Hospital currently has 1,500 wounded soldiers. Sometimes, the required supplies are not delivered in time, and the local government temporarily makes advance payments. The Ministry of Military Affairs telegraphed the county government to settle the advance payments within two days, and the vouchers must be claimed back within ten days.

Method for Distributing and Subscribing Customs Treasury Bonds: Tongyi was assigned 40,000 yuan of customs treasury bonds. After deliberations by representatives from all sectors, it was decided to raise 13,000 yuan first: 3,000 yuan subscribed by the industrial sector, 5,500 yuan by the commercial sector, and 4,500 yuan by wealthy individuals in each district.

Jiading

Investigating the Case of a Porter Beating Someone to Death: A case of a porter beating someone to death occurred at Anting Station on the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway. On the 23rd of last month, the county government opened a court to investigate. The wife of the deceased, Fu Wang, testified that her husband was fatally beaten by Luo Jinzhang, a porter at the station. Luo has been detained. In order to clarify the case, the Shanghai Railway Administration dispatched Wang Shuchun, the head of the Eastern Section of the Transportation Department, to Anting yesterday (the 2nd) to inquire about the truth from the district office and to interview people in the villages near the station to avoid any miscarriage of justice. It is reported that Chief Wang has obtained accurate information and will report it truthfully.

Penalties for Purchasing Stolen Rice: At the end of last month, a rice shop on Huangdu Town Main Street in the 6th district of the county purchased 220 packages of Xian rice from a Pudong boatman hired to transport grain for a cheap price of eight yuan per package (or 1,500 yuan in total). It turned out that the glazed rice was loaded by a Shanghai shipping company and transported out of the North Station. After discovering the theft, the thief was reported to the police for investigation. A certain Chinese detective arrested the boatman, who confessed to the theft and pointed out the address and name of the buyer. The jurisdictional authority prepared a document to transfer and interrogate him. He confessed to mistakenly buying stolen goods and was sentenced to compensate for the price of the rice, a fine of 4,000 yuan, and a seven-month prison sentence. The shop owner sought bail to return to his hometown and is now raising funds to pay the fine and seeking ways to atone for his crime.

Xiaoshan

Execution of Accomplice Zhong Ama by Firing Squad: On the 31st, the Xiaoshan County Government approved the transfer of Zhong Ama, an accomplice sent by the Provincial Public Security Bureau. He was from Shangbao, Qibu in the southern countryside. In March of last year, he gathered hundreds of people to forcibly cut bamboo and trees on Zhong Lingqiu's mountain, and was arrested by the county. Due to the seriousness of the case, he was transferred to the provincial government for interrogation. After the provincial government found out that the suspect was performing important duties for the rebellious party, he was sentenced to death and secretly ordered the Provincial Public Security Bureau to send personnel to Xiaoshan to execute him on the spot yesterday morning.

Construction of County Roads Begins: The first phase of the construction of Xiaoshan County Road, starting from outside the West Gate and ending at Xixing New Bridge, has been contracted out to merchants through bidding. The contract was signed, and construction began today (the 1st). At 8 AM, a commencement ceremony was held at Caolin Temple outside the West Gate, with representatives from various agencies and organizations attending.

Meeting on Methods for Collecting Stored Grain Donations: The Xiaoshan County Government convened a temporary meeting at the county government at 2 PM on August 29 to discuss the donation rate for the approved collection of stored grain donations for disaster relief. The resolution from the second administrative meeting was whether or not to differentiate the annual donation of one jiao per mu for all fields, lands, and mountain ponds. It was resolved that there would be no distinction for fields and lands, and the levy would remain at one jiao per mu, while mountain ponds would be changed to a levy of three fen per mu.

Hefei

Confiscation of Illegally Transported Military Weapons: The head of the Joint Military and Police Inspection Office, Wei Xuwu, reported that on the 28th, Li's team captured two criminals, Li Buzhou and Huang Yongfu, who were illegally transporting military weapons in a civilian boat in Sanhe. They seized 21 Mauser rifles and tens of thousands of rounds of ammunition, and escorted them back to the inspection office. Deputy Director Yang interrogated Li, who stated that he was the captain of the Sanhe Town Merchants Team and that he and Huang had purchased the weapons at Zhongxingji for use. The Inspection Office, considering the seriousness of the case, transferred it to the 6th District Bandit Suppression Headquarters for handling. Also, the Inspection Office arrested Ye Tingyu, who was impersonating an inspector to extort money, at Daifu's residence today. He was severely punished with a thousand lashes and expelled from the area.

The Second Brigade Cancelled: More than 200 bandits led by Guo Wuleizi in the southwest countryside were previously recruited by former County Magistrate Wang Peishi and organized into the Second Guerrilla Brigade, appointing Zhang Huaikang as the captain. They were ordered to be stationed near Huanghuadun for training. Since Wang's departure, the local government has largely denied them, leading to difficulties in supplying them. Currently, as a certain unit in Lu'an is recruiting soldiers in the western countryside, the brigade has also turned to that unit to pledge allegiance, and negotiations are nearly complete. The Hefei County Government has approved the cancellation of the Second Brigade, and the brigade commander Zhang Huaikang has also been relieved of his post.

Letter

Letter From the Shandong Salt Transport Office

Our office received a telegram from the Ministry of Finance in June, approving General He's telegram from Xuzhou stating that people on the Shandong border were suffering due to difficulty in selling salt. We were instructed to investigate and respond. We followed orders and sent commissioners to Xuzhou to investigate in detail. We also heard that the Luchang Company had illegal practices that harmed the people. We instructed the commissioners to investigate this matter as well. Subsequently, we received a report from the Xuzhou Inspection Bureau stating that on July 13, the Ji Yu Company transported 5,772 dan of salt that should have been sold in the Guide nine prefectures to the Luchang Company without authorization. They only reported the inspection after unloading the salt, violating the regulations. They were not inspected, detained, and reported for instructions. We also received a report from the commissioner to Xuzhou stating that they learned in Haizhou that a batch of salt from the Ji Yu Company bound for Henan had already been transported and unloaded in Xuzhou. They immediately consulted with the Inspection Bureau and learned that 1,872 dan had been unloaded and handed over to the Luchang Company. They then went to Luchang to inquire and were told that the salt was sealed in the warehouse, but those involved had left and could not be inspected. Suspecting the words were evasive, they went to the warehouse to inspect and found many suspicious points. They immediately sealed it with the Inspection Bureau. On July 13, they went to the Luchang main warehouse to check the accounts and suddenly saw a large amount of salt piled up. When they questioned the manager, they avoided them. After repeated investigations, they learned that this was the second batch of 5,772 dan delivered to Luchang by the Ji Yu Company, and they did not report it for inspection in accordance with the regulations. They immediately telegraphed the Inspection Bureau for instructions. The transporter, knowing that it had been discovered, sent a servant with a permit to request inspection, which was rejected by the Inspection Bureau, stating that the salt had been unloaded privately and could not be inspected. They should wait for instructions and follow them. At the same time, they ordered the Luchang Company to be responsible for the safekeeping. It was found that the Ji Yu Company was approved to sell 10,000 dan in Xuzhou last year, and it had already been transported. Now, when reporting the first batch arriving in Xuzhou, they dared to claim approval for selling in Xuzhou. The second batch was not reported for inspection, but was unloaded privately and piled up in Luchang, which was obviously colluding for illegal sales, and there was no guarantee that there was no private involvement. Salt that had not been approved for sale and violated inspection regulations should be treated as illegal salt according to regulations. The company dared to collude and attempt, which was truly reckless. The recent salt shortage in Xuzhou was indeed true, and it was due to Luchang's inability to raise funds to lead and supply salt, only knowing how to collect private profits. They repeatedly refused to hand over the account books for inspection, and the amount of stored salt was kept secret. Accepting and storing the illegal salt of the Ji Yu Company was also evidence of their private profiteering. According to the salt price regulations, Tongshan was 8.35 cents per catty, but Luchang raised the price to over 1 jiao. Xiaoxian was 8.85 cents per catty, but Luchang raised the price to 1 jiao and 3 li. Small vendors also raised the price to as much as 1 jiao and 5 fen. The salt scale was also short by about 13 taels per catty. All kinds of malpractices caused the people to suffer. The above-mentioned situations were all personally investigated by the official commissioners, who verified the prices, sought opinions, and all agreed. We should first report the details of the investigation to the Salt Department, and ask whether the illegal salt of the Ji Yu Company should be confiscated and fined in accordance with regulations, and how the malpractice of the Luchang Company should be strictly punished according to law. We await your instructions. After receiving the report, we ordered the Luchang Company to suspend business temporarily and await investigation. At the same time, we telegraphed the Ministry of Finance for review, and we immediately received a telegram instructing us to confiscate all the seized salt and to draft a plan for punishing the Luchang Company and submit it for approval. The above is the process of the confiscation of the Ji Yu Company's salt. Afterwards, the company falsely reported to the Ministry of Finance that it was an illegal punishment because it had failed to bribe. General He turned it into the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Finance issued it to our office. The company's illegal actions were unknown, and they turned to slander. The facts were not confused because of this, and the law was responsible. Since the company has published a telegram in the newspaper, it is specially disclosed to clarify the truth.

Schools Are Not Allowed to Accommodate Outsiders

The Capital Garrison Command Instructs the Ministry to Relay to its Affiliates

Riri News Beijing Dispatch: The Capital Garrison Command believes that during holidays, schools at all levels often have outsiders lodging in them. At a time when strict precautions are being taken against Communist Party members and other reactionary elements lurking in various places, there is a risk of negligence. Yesterday, the command sent a special letter to the Ministry of Education, requesting that all schools at all levels strictly refuse outsiders to lodge in order to prevent them from becoming havens for reactionary elements. It is reported that the Ministry of Education has prepared to instruct all its affiliates to comply and eliminate reactionary elements.

The Ministry of Education Commends the Liaoning Education Department

For Paying Attention to Library Development

The Ministry of Education previously instructed the Liaoning Provincial Education Department to diligently implement the various articles submitted by the China Library Association. According to the subsequent report (1) (Instructing all levels of schools to stipulate book purchase fees) all levels of schools have been notified to comply and provincial schools are allowed to use half of the tuition income for book purchases. (2) (Increasing the number of various libraries) It is planned to increase a public library in the provincial capital in the 19th year. The counties have been notified to actively prepare for the increase. (3) (Hiring experts to guide library development) It is planned to convene library staff from various counties to the province during the winter vacation to organize library science workshops and hire library science experts to lecture and guide them. (4) (Recruiting library science students to study abroad) When the students sent by the province graduate and return to the country, one library science student will be selected for overseas study. Recently, one or two librarians from the provincial library have been selected to study library science at domestic universities. (5) (Reducing the price of publications from educational institutions) The pricing of publications from the department has been reduced and all departments have been notified to comply. (6) (Instructing all universities to set up library science courses to become library science departments) Northeast University and Fengyong University have been notified to consider this matter. All the details of compliance have been reported in writing for review. The Ministry of Education recently issued the following instructions to the department: "We have received the report. We commend the department for its important and commendable report on its compliance with the various articles. We still hope that you will report the progress of the development of library development at any time for future reference."

The Ministry of Education Orders the Disbandment of the Female Affiliated Middle School of Peiping University

The Ministry of Education received a telegram from the student union of the Female Affiliated Middle School of Peiping University stating that the school opened as scheduled today, with 259 returning students and 89 new students. The Ministry of Education, believing that the school was defying the ministry's orders, telegraphed Peiping University yesterday to investigate and disband the school. The original telegram stated: "Peiping University, we have received your Female Affiliated Middle School's East Telegram stating that the school has been ordered to unconditionally transfer to the Female Normal College before the end of July. If you resist the order, you will be disbanded. We have now received an East Telegram from the school's student union stating that the affiliated school opened as scheduled today. This is obviously defying the ministry's orders. We order you to investigate and disband the school. Ministry of Education, Winter Seal."

Professor Renor's Mission to China

To Make New Contributions to the Economy of the New China Era

Arriving in China on the Russian Empress, Expected to Arrive at Port Tomorrow

(China Foreign News International News) In recent years, foreigners studying Oriental issues have paid special attention to economic and commercial aspects. For example, Adans's study of railway accounting in our country, Johnson's investigation of transportation issues, and our government's hiring of foreign experts are not uncommon. For example, the hiring of Jingqi and Huishilin during the late Qing Dynasty and the establishment of the Kemal Design Committee in recent times.

Among the guest professors, apart from Adans, Professor Renor has made considerable contributions to the academic world in our country. His books, such as Lectures on China's International Trade Economy, have had a great impact on the economic circles in our country. This time, in addition to studying China's international finance and economy, he will also visit major commercial ports in our country. This trip is commissioned by the New York Institute of Social Sciences and the Advisory Committee of the Brookings Institution (Washington). It has been two years since the Institute of Social Sciences passed his proposal in the summer of the 17th year of the Republic of China.

Last year's Pacific National Conference in Nishikyo, Japan, devoted a major part of its program to the issue of foreign investment in China. At that time, the various reports on this category included the following:

Foreign Investment in China: Liu Dajun

British Investment in China: Committee of the Royal Institute of International Affairs

Japanese Investment in China: Ri Wotian Jue

French and German Investment in China: Professor Elice (University of Michigan)

American Investment in China: Professor Renor

Comparing the number of investments in China by various powers, there are discrepancies. Therefore, correcting these differences is also an important issue in the future. As a result, the total amount of investment in China by the powers will be accurate. The important part of the total includes the national debt of the national government. This issue was paid attention to by the Kemal Design Committee last year, and Professor Kai's investigation made the total amount of national debt of the national government clearer.

Professor Lei's research has shown that the direct investment in China by foreign stores far exceeds the national debt of the national government, and the amount may be several times greater. It is extremely difficult to calculate this type of direct investment. Therefore, the importance of foreign direct investment and the results of investment in China by the powers is obvious. In addition, the impact of foreign investment in China on our people's economic, political, and social life is also a key point of this research. Moreover, attention is also paid to our country's economic system under the treaty port system and extraterritoriality.

In addition, the amount of investment in the country by overseas Chinese in Nanyang is also a topic of research for the professor. Unfortunately, the remittance system is simple and there is no way to start the investigation. The banks in Shanghai are also unwilling to show their internal situation to others. It is heard that the National Jinan University in West Shanghai has established a South Ocean and American Cultural Business Department. The person in charge is deeply aware of the overseas Chinese situation and may be able to help.

Professor Lei will arrive in Shanghai on the Russian Empress on September 5th. Several young economists will come with him.

Preparatory Office Distributes Annual Meeting Guide

Deadline for Registration and Train Arrangements

The Ministry of Education previously announced that the deadline for submissions for the national anthem was the end of August. It has received approximately 700 submissions. Local News

Reopening of Quanzhou-Zhangzhou Middle School

Approved by the Municipal Government Yesterday

And Ordered the School to Thoroughly Rectify

The Daily News reports that the Quanzhou-Zhangzhou Middle School on Longhua Road in this city was sealed up more than a year ago because students were propagating reactionary ideas. It is now reported that the school's board of directors has decided to continue operating the school and to thoroughly rectify it. Yesterday, they appointed representatives, including Zhuang Yizhong, to petition the Municipal Government to allow the school to reopen. Yesterday, the Municipal Government approved the reopening, stating that the school site is originally the property of the guild hall. Since the appointed representatives have requested the reopening, it should be approved. However, the school was previously sealed because the students' propagation of reactionary ideas was a serious offense. Now that it is proposed to reopen, the school should immediately adhere to the methods instructed by the Education Bureau, properly reorganize, and thoroughly rectify the school. In addition to ordering the Public Security and Education Bureaus, the school must comply with these instructions.

Internal Reforms at Soochow University Law School

Since Dr. Wu Jingxiong and Dr. Sheng Zhenwei became presidents of the Soochow University Law School on Kunshan Road, they have made more reforms internally in order to suit the study of law based on individual aptitude and talent, especially in the area of Chinese law. Renovation of the Shanghai Art College

Since the selection of a large open space in front of the Tiantong'an Railway Station on Zhabei Wan Road to build a magnificent school building, it has been gradually completed recently. It is now scheduled to open on the 5th of this month, and a ceremony will be held at the same time to celebrate the completion of the new school building. In the Western Painting Department, in addition to Principal Wang Daoyuan serving as a professor and Zhu Yingpeng, a member of the school's basic committee, serving as a professor of theory, the famous painter Chen Baoyi and the new-style writer Ni Hua, who recently returned to Shanghai from Guangdong, have also been newly hired as Western painting professors. The pattern painter Chen Zhifo will serve as a professor of pattern design and theory. In the Music Department, in addition to the Director of Studies, Shen Jilu, serving concurrently, and Tan Shuzhen, a former member of the school's basic committee, serving as a professor of violin, You Wenmo and Yu Yuezhang have also been newly hired to serve as piano professors.

Vocational Education Society Cultivates Talents for Industry and Commerce

Recently, the China Vocational Education Society has been meeting the needs of municipal organizations and the business community for clerical personnel. For example, the clerical workers and Chinese typists used by the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Finance, Bureau of Social Affairs, Bureau of Public Safety, Bureau of Public Works, Bureau of Public Utilities, Bank of China, and Shanghai Bank are all graduates of the Society's night school. Therefore, the Society is continuing to offer a special course in clerical work, which focuses on Chinese typing in addition to clerical work, file management, statistics, and shorthand. Mr. Song Mingde, director of the Chinese Typing Department of the Commercial Press, will continue to be in charge of teaching. In addition, in order to meet the needs of various organizations that entrust the Society to find personnel, who must be proficient in daily English, and to facilitate the supplementary study of service personnel in various organizations, a daily English course has been added. Furthermore, after the Ministry of Industry and Commerce issued the outline of the worker education plan, all factories must carry out worker education but are worried about the lack of teachers. The Society has therefore established a teacher training program for worker education, focusing on worker education facilities, teaching methods, factory equipment and safety, scientific management, and industrial and commercial laws. The Society has sent letters to the Shanghai Machinery National Goods Factory Federation, notifying the factories to send factory employees to the school for study. Currently, enrollments in all courses are extremely enthusiastic and will soon be full. The entrance examination is scheduled to be held on the 7th of this month.

Guangdong Tianma Result Winner

Luo Hongsheng Lu Hanjun 3-0 Guangdong

Deng Guofu Ma Tingliang 3-0 Guangdong

Lu Zhongqiu Sun Jianqu 3-0 Guangdong

Huang Anbang Lu Shentong 1-3 Tianma

Huang Xiangfa Zhu Guisheng 3-0 Guangdong

Commentary on the Skills: Luo Hongsheng vs. Lu Hanjun: Mr. Luo is a veteran with long experience, having attended the Far Eastern Games. He is good at defense and precise strokes. Mr. Lu is a young and handsome man who is brave and good at fighting. Although his offense and defense are appropriate, he lacks experience, which led to his defeat. Deng Guofu is a newly emerging talent, but he is diligent in practice and his strokes are powerful. Although Ma has been on the battlefield for a long time and is good at defending, he was unable to cope with the attacks and was defeated. Lu Zhongqiu is an athlete who attended the Far Eastern Games and defeated Morita of Japan. He has excellent technique, is good at counterattacks, and injects when he sees an opportunity. Although Mr. Sun actively resisted, he was eventually defeated due to lack of time to care for all areas. Huang Anbang is one of the new generals, with precise strokes. Lu Shentong is excellent in both long-range and close-range attacks, and his technique is superior. The audience was most excited and he won against Huang by a score of three to one. Huang Xiangfa is a representative to the Far Eastern Games for the second time and is the most experienced among the competitors, with the best defense. Although Zhu is good at strokes and defense, he eventually found it difficult to cope. He used strokes, which were exceptionally powerful, and Huang sometimes could not cope, but Zhu often committed suicide. Huang was more stable, so the victory belonged to Huang.

Local News

Circulation of Rice and Grain from Various Provinces

Good News for the People's Food Problem

Jiangxi Rice Also Lifted: The Jiangxi Provincial Government believes that this year's harvest in Jiangxi Province is very abundant. In addition to supplying the people's food in the province, there is surplus rice that can be exported. It was decided to follow the example of Hunan rice leaving the country. From September 1st, Jiangxi rice will also be allowed to be purchased by other provinces, with Jiujiang as the port for transit and exit. Rice merchants in Shanghai have already sent telegrams to Jiangxi to purchase and transport rice. A large batch of Jiangxi rice will arrive in Shanghai next week.

Hunan Rice Continues to Arrive: Since the lifting of the ban on Hunan rice, many batches have arrived in Shanghai. In the past two days, batches continued to be loaded from Changsha to Hankou and transferred to Shanghai, totaling two batches, one with 800 bags and one with 3,097 bags. Yesterday, they were all unloaded in this city, one stored in the Hongkou godown and one unloaded in Puxi. It is reported that there are still more than 10,000 bags that will be imported in the next few days.

No Obstruction to Rice Leaving Tianjin: Tianjin has come to Shanghai to purchase rice, but the Jianghai Customs has banned transportation for two weeks. Subsequently, due to the issue of people's food and the fact that most of the rice purchased was foreign rice, the ban was lifted. Recently, there has been no obstruction to the transportation of rice and grain from Shanghai to Tianjin. Local Chinese steamships are all loading.

The Impending Sino-Japanese Telecommunications Negotiations

News From the Japanese Side

Regarding the Sino-Japanese telecommunications negotiations, the diplomatic authorities of the two countries have officially appointed the negotiators, and all the procedures have been agreed upon by the Japanese Acting Minister Chong Guang Kui and Foreign Minister Wang. Therefore, formal negotiations can begin soon. A reporter from the Guowen News Agency visited the Japanese Embassy office yesterday and obtained the following news:

Japanese Negotiators: The Japanese government attaches great importance to these telecommunications negotiations. In addition to appointing Acting Minister Chong Guang Kui as the chairman of the committee to take overall charge, the Director of the Savings Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, Yoshino Keizo, has also been appointed as a specialist committee member. Mr. Yoshino once served as the Chief of the Overseas Telecommunications Section of the Ministry of Communications and is the foremost expert in Japan on overseas telecommunications. It has now been confirmed that he will come to Shanghai on the 10th of this month. The Japanese government yesterday also ordered the Secretary of the Ministry of Communications, Iino Takeo, to be the Secretary-General, and Mori Kanji and Makabe Sanzaburo of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to be secretaries. They will all come to Shanghai on the same ship with Director Yoshino on the 10th of this month.

Scope of Negotiations: According to an investigation, in addition to the submarine cable from Shanghai to Nagasaki, the Japanese have established several telegraph lines in China, including Fuzhou-Taiwan, Dalian-Zhifu, and Dalian-Guozheng Island. These are all submarine cables, and the Chinese and Japanese governments have treaties with each other. Therefore, the scope of future negotiations will be based on the above lines.

Prospects for Negotiations: According to news from the Japanese side, the National Government's communications authorities are eager to recover the telecommunications established by foreigners in China. Foreign Minister Wang and Communications Minister Wang have repeatedly held informal discussions and private meetings with the Japanese Acting Minister Chong Guang Kui. Although they have come close, the Japanese government's planned plan is quite different from the National Government's opinion. Therefore, there will inevitably be many twists and turns after the negotiations begin. Although the treaty may be revised, it is difficult to predict the date of the establishment of a new treaty.

Date of Commencement of Negotiations: Chong Guang Kui told a reporter from the Guowen News Agency yesterday that Director Yoshino has been scheduled to come to Shanghai around the 10th of this month and will arrive in Shanghai by the 15th at the latest. The Chinese Ministry of Communications authorities have also prepared all the procedures. Therefore, the formal negotiation meeting will be held by the 20th of this month at the latest. The meeting place will be in the capital, and I will personally go to Beijing for the meeting at that time.
