Reasons for Increasing Fees for Purchasing Passenger Clearance and Cargo Discharge Permits

Reply from the Inspector General of Customs to the Shipping Association

The Shanghai Shipping Association previously received letters from member companies stating that the Customs had received an order from the Inspector General of Customs to uniformly increase the fees for purchasing passenger clearance and cargo discharge permits by 80% after 6:00 PM and on Sundays and holidays from the 16th of this month. After receiving the letter, the Shipping Association sent a letter to the Inspector General of Customs Public Office, requesting the revocation of the order. Yesterday, the Inspector General of Customs Public Office replied to the Shipping Association, "In reply, we have received your association's letter No. 70, stating that member companies have received a customs notice saying that it has received an order from the Inspector General of Customs, instructing to uniformly increase the fee by eighty percent for purchasing passenger clearance and cargo discharge permits for all ships after six o'clock and on Sundays and holidays starting from September sixteenth. We are really not able to shoulder the expense and plead for you to represent us in sincerely asking that the order be withdrawn in order for us to eke out a living. We have investigated what you have stated and what you said is indeed the case and we urgently report the situation for your perusal so that the previous order for increasing the fees is rescinded in order to aid our difficulties and maintain the shipping business etcetera. Having given these matters our consideration, we are explaining to your association the reasons for our decision to increase the permit fees so that all shipowners will understand that our office increasing the fees is really not something we did willingly. The amount of special permit fees that we currently collect is the same as it was sixty years ago. Back then, the fee was sufficient to cover the Customs’ expenses for all the overtime work done during evenings, Sundays, and public holidays, so the regulations were considered reasonable then, but now sixty years have passed. In these sixty years, prices have soared, and they continue to rise. Taking the average price of a year ago, prices have increased by two or three times compared with the tenth year of the Tongzhi reign, so the Customs’ expenses have increased similarly, but the special permit fees have not been increased once. The drop in the price of silver last year caused prices to rise further to a point where they were double those of last year, and the current price is about six times higher than it was sixty years ago. In this situation, where fees for the transshipment of goods, ship water fees, and delay fees have increased, it is difficult for the Customs to continue to use the previous regulations for these permits without increasing them appropriately. The Customs could reduce the number of staff it needs to reduce expenses if it were to cancel the convenience of ships being able to load and unload goods at night or on holidays, but this would have a large impact on business, so we have given the matter much consideration and determined that the only way to proceed is to increase the permit fees so that the additional fees can contribute to the expense that the additional workload necessitates. The increase has been decided to be eighty percent. If one were to think carefully about how prices have increased over the last sixty years, one could not say that the amount is too high. Furthermore, the amount of delay fees set by the various shipping companies is much higher than it was sixty years ago. In the future, when the permit fee has increased to eighteen taels, if the shipowners pay the fee according to the set amount, the ship will not be delayed, and the expenses saved on delay fees will be greater than the ten taels that would have been saved sixty years ago, so it is only natural that the Customs increase the special permit fee. Moreover, the Customs increasing the special permit fee is different from increasing tariffs or tonnage duties, because an increase in tariffs and tonnage duties means that ship owners and shippers have no choice but to pay the fees while shipowners are free to choose whether to purchase a special permit or not. The Customs is not compelling merchants to purchase the special permit, and if merchants think that the fee is too high and they would rather delay the shipping of goods than purchase the special permit, the Customs is happy to allow them to do so and will not interfere in their decision. In short, our office is always concerned about the difficult situation facing merchants and will do everything in our power to alleviate the difficulties. However, this increase in the special permit fee is due to the aforementioned unavoidable circumstances. It is hoped that domestic war will end and business will return to normal by next month (September) the increase in the permit fee takes effect on September the sixteenth. We are responding to the letter that you have sent and hope that you will investigate this matter. After receiving the letter, the association copied the original letter and sent it to its member companies for reference.

Director Wu of the Construction Bureau Discusses the Situation of the Minping Road

The National Road Association plans to build a highway from Minhang in Shanghai to Pinghu in Zhejiang Province as a commemorative road for the association's tenth anniversary. The Shanghai County Government has already issued instructions to the Construction Bureau to prepare a plan. Director Wu has sent people to investigate and solicit opinions from Jinshan, Fengxian, and Pinghu counties and reported the situation to the county government, which has replied to the association. Director Wu gave a detailed account of the surveyed route yesterday, stating that there are approximately two routes in general: (1) Ferrying from Minhang south to Punan, passing through Nanqiao and Zhalin, then turning west along the sea dike to Pinghu. This route is about four li from the ferry to Punan and then south to Xiaotang in the territory of Taiping Township, Nanhui County. It is said that construction is scheduled to begin after autumn this year. It is twelve li from Xiaotang south to Nanqiao. The roadbed has been completed by the Fengxian County Construction Bureau in the eighteenth year of the Republic of China, and the plans for bridges and culverts have also been drafted and are scheduled to be constructed within the year. However, it is unlikely that the approximately seventeen li section from Nanqiao to Zhalin will be built in the short term. From Zhalin, turning west, passing through Hequekou, Jinshanzui, Jinshanwei, Xugongting, and other places, is approximately more than fifty li. The original sea dike can be used. From Xugongting, northwest, passing through Zhao Jiaqiao, Zhou Jiaxu Zhen, and other towns in Pinghu, to reach Pinghu, is 46 li. The advantages of this route are: (1) The Minnan Road can be used; (2) the sea dike, bridges, and culverts can be used, and the land price can be saved. It is estimated that only the 17 li from Nanqiao to Zhalin and the 46 li from Xugongting to Pinghu, a total of 60 li, need to be built. However, there are also three disadvantages: (1) The route is 130 li long; (2) the route is a large arc; (3) there are few prosperous towns along the way, and the output of grain, cotton, etc., is less than that of fish and salt, making it difficult to develop business. (2) From Minhang to Nanqiao, turning west, passing through Zhuanghang, Tinglin and Zhangyan, which are under the jurisdiction of Songjiang County, and Qinwangshan and other towns, which are under the jurisdiction of Jinshan County, to reach the east gate of Pinghu. This route is the same as the first route from Minhang to Nanqiao. From Nanqiao, turning west and passing through Zhuanghang to Yandun Zhen is more than 31 li, which is under the jurisdiction of Fengxian County. From Yandun Zhen, crossing the Longquan Port (river width is about 20 meters) into the territory of Songjiang County, six li southwest is Tinglin Zhen. Fourteen li south is Zhangyan Zhen, crossing Zhangjing in the west of the town into the territory of Jinshan County. Sixteen li to the southwest, passing the north of Qinwang Mountain, to Xinmiao Zhen, which is under the jurisdiction of Pinghu County. 11 more li west is Guangchen Zhen, which is the place with the lowest terrain in Pingfeng (there are many lakes and swamps, making construction difficult). 25 more li west is the east gate of Pinghu County. The advantages of this route are: (1) The Minnan Line can be used; (2) the route is more direct, the total length is 110 li, which is 20 li less than the first line; (3) There are many prosperous cities and towns along the way, and there is an abundance of cotton and rice, so business should be more developed. As for the disadvantages, there are more bridges and culverts, and there is nothing to borrow except for the Minnan Line, so everything must be built, and the land price and construction costs are huge. The above two routes have their own advantages and disadvantages. However, the cost plan and other items must first clarify the width of the road surface and the type of road surface, and then make an approximate estimate. If you want an accurate budget, you must also understand the land price in each place, the type of bridge, and carry out a precise survey before you can make a plan for use as a standard. The route passes through Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, and those in the Jiangsu boundary must pass through Nanhui, Fengxian, Songjiang, and Jinshan counties. Unless the two provinces are consulted by letter and special commissioners are organized to form a surveying team, it will be difficult to gather things. Although the starting point of the selected route is in Shanghai, the place it passes through is all in dangerous terrain. Therefore, when our bureau sent personnel to investigate, we deeply felt that the authority was not within our scope, and there were many obstacles.

New Product: Gramophone Oil

Gramophones come in double-spring and single-spring varieties, but after prolonged use, they often develop a rattling sound inside, and the movement becomes sluggish, uneven in speed, and prone to mainspring breakage or gear damage (if excessively thick, gummy oil is used, the parts can become greasy; if too thin and fluid, lubrication is inadequate). The Sheep Brand dual-purpose oil for gramophones and records, newly invented by the Anquan Trading Company of Weian Lane, Hai Ning Road, this city, ensures smooth operation when dripped into the mechanism. Gears and springs are also protected from breakage. Recently, records are being played with electric pickups, resulting in exceptionally loud and clear sound and timbre. However, prolonged playing can cause white lines to appear on the record, or the stylus may drag or become stuck, or even lose the original sound. It is best to avoid overly thick, greasy oil or excessively thin, fluid oil. Sheep Brand dual-purpose oil should be used for wiping, which can remove even the finest dust and restore old records. This oil has been refined using scientific methods to achieve the ideal thickness, drying easily without leaving a greasy residue, resulting in the special effectiveness described above. It is an essential product for those who own gramophones and records. The price is also affordable, at only six jiao per bottle. It is available at Yong'an, Lihua, Xin Sheng, Xin Sheng, Kuaile, Fuji, Zhongguo, Sanxing, Shanghai Tianxing, Tianle, and other gramophone companies in this city, as well as Longji in Tianjin, Longji in Beiping, Yongzi in Hankou, Da Chang Cheng, Lin Yuanfeng in Shantou, and Huadeli in Wuxi. To show their appreciation to customers, the company offers free postage for direct mail orders. They are also recruiting distributors in various ports.

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs Adopts Qu's Telegraph Code Method

Qu Chongfu, a master's degree holder who studied abroad, has extensive experience in cataloging. He has always felt that our country's telegraphic code checking is complicated and difficult, which is not only time-consuming but also prone to errors. He finally succeeded in creating a special method. The basic strokes of his checking method only have ten major parts, unlike the old method where each character must be painstakingly searched for in the two hundred and fourteen letters. Any person can learn this checking method in just five minutes. The newly compiled "Qu's Telegraph Code Checking" book was first approved by Hu Shi, He Lu, and Gu Shusen. Furthermore, at the National Library Association in the capital last year, one hundred and seventy-odd library experts publicly tested the method, and the result was that each character only required five seconds to check. Yuan Tongli, chairman of the association, and Dai Zhichou, the current president, both certified and signed that it eliminates previous complexities and provides convenience to society. Yesterday, the Telegraph Section of the General Affairs Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the National Government in Nanjing sent a letter to Mr. Qu, excerpted below: "Mr. Chongfu, greetings. Since you invented the telegraph code checking method, users have praised its convenience. Our ministry has been revising the telegraph book. After much consideration regarding the checking method, we have finally decided to adopt your method. If you agree, please reply so that we can proceed. Furthermore, we plan to inquire at any time if we encounter difficulties. We hope that you will not hesitate to give us your advice. Sincerely, the Telegraph Section of the General Affairs Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs." It is said that there are not many copies of the newly published "Qu's Telegraph Code Checking" book left. Those who want to see it first can order it from the Qu's Telegraph Code Checking Company, the general distributor at No. 62 Jiangxi Road, this city.

YMCA Promotes Harmonicas

The Shanghai YMCA believes that harmonica music is suitable for the entertainment of the Chinese people and urgently needs to be promoted. It can be learned in two months with twice a week lessons. At the same time, a (Harmonica Team) is also attached so that those who are proficient in this technique can join the research at any time (still under the guidance of Mr. Wang). The fees are very low. It is currently recruiting male and female members. Anyone who loves to study harmonica, regardless of whether they are beginners or advanced learners, regardless of gender, can register at the Shanghai YMCA Office on Sichuan Road starting today. The deadline is September 11.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Mediates Wine Guild's Seizure of Wine Case

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce previously received a letter from the Soy Sauce and Wine Industry Association, stating that the Shaoxing Wine Guild had arbitrarily seized Suzhou wine, hindering business, and requested the Chamber of Commerce to preside over the investigation. The Chamber of Commerce then convened a meeting of the Wine Industry Association and the Soy Sauce and Wine Industry Association for mediation. All the seized wine should be returned to the original owners by the Shaoxing Wine Association. At the same time, the following mediation measures were formulated: (1) Suzhou wine arriving in Shanghai should be freely bought and sold directly by wine and soy sauce merchants, and should not be interfered with by the Shaoxing Wine Association. (2) The Shaoxing Wine Association guarantees that such behavior will not happen again in the future. (3) Suzhou wine arriving in Shanghai should be handled in the same way as the majority, and no excessive fees should be charged, etc. Yesterday, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce reported the mediation process to the Social Affairs Bureau for record.

Students (in unison): Teacher, we can have a two or three-day vacation.

Servant: Madam, it's just that I can't find the feather duster. There's no way to dust off the dust. So I sat in the chair one by one. So the dust is gone, isn't it?

Quack doctor: You don't believe in my self-made medicine? But for twenty years, I don't know how much I've sold. The people who take the medicine have never said a bad word.

Patient: The dead naturally won't open their mouths.

Criminal: When they caught me that day. I fought five policemen alone. I hit them so hard that their heads were bleeding. Isn't that considered a struggle?

Record of the Wang Family Heirloom in Dongting Mountain

— Juemi

The Wang family should be the first in the Dongting Mountain family. The Wang family has lived in Dongting Mountain for the longest time. And since the Song Dynasty. There are Fu people in every generation. Just like Wang Ao, a famous minister of the former Ming Dynasty, was also a native of Dongting Mountain. Wang Ao's character is Jiaxi. Died with the posthumous title of Wenk. When Wenke was in court. There is a picture of going to court with difficulty. After returning home. There is a picture of Hezhou. After his death. There is also a picture of five similarities. These three pictures are actually the Wang family heirloom in Dongting Mountain today. The picture of going to court. Painting the scene of Wenke going to court. What is painted. The palace is above. Wenke is below. Wenke is wearing court clothes and court crown. Holding the Hu to go to court. So in Wenke. But draw its back. And the dignified and respectful demeanor of the ancient ministers can be obtained from its back. Hezhou map. Painting the scene of Wenke boating in the mountains and valleys after returning home. After Wenke returned home. He often travels among the mountains and valleys or boats in the valleys. So Wenke was painted as a Hezhou map. When Wenke died. Several were at the same time as Wenke. The same imperial examination. The same official rank. The same title. The same Bright Festival. Those with the same posthumous title. There are five people. So five people including Wenke were painted as five similar pictures. At this point, three pictures. One is a vertical axis. One is a booklet page. One is a hand scroll. The two pictures of going to court and five similarities. There is no Kuan Zhi. The Hezhou map is from the hands of Shen Qinan, the first painter of the former Ming Dynasty. These three. Pictures Ming and Qing dynasties famous ministers and ministers. And the great poets. Great essayists. What great poets and essayists wrote. Each has seventy or eighty families. It is said that the masters of the Ming and Qing dynasties. The net is exhausted. Lu Fengshi Runxiang, Minister of the Qing Dynasty. In fact, he is the house of the Wang family. Therefore, the Hezhou map is titled. It is also enshrined in Fengshi. Fengshi has been to Wang's house in person after being noble. Seeing the picture and writing it, Fengshi even got to see this picture at that time. Cited as a lifelong blessing. To Qian Yinren specifically carved the four-character seal of Fengshi's eye blessing. Qian Qi Bo is behind him. It is also possible to know the preciousness of this picture. Now these three pictures are kept in each room of the Wang family. I refuse to show it to people easily. So even Wenke's descendants. Not easy to see. My friend Mr. Wang Shushan is a descendant of Wenke. It is also said that he has only seen two pictures of going to court and Hezhou in his life. I have not seen the five same pictures. The Wang family has a regular sacrifice every spring. That is, it is held at the Dongting Mountain Ancestral Hall. Those of the descendants who arrive. Each sign on the name book. This name book has been preserved since the Yuan and Ming dynasties. No omissions. Accumulate to hundreds of copies. The Wang family also regards it as a Fu family heirloom.

The Sparrow Fever in Tokyo

— Ai Ai sent from Japan

Sparrows in Japan. It is really at its peak for a while. Not to mention other prefectures and counties. Tokyo City alone. There are now more than 1,100 mahjong clubs. Colorful door lights painted with beautiful women's faces and bright flags. The glittering sign. Almost on every street. There are always a few mahjong clubs that come into contact with people's eyes.

In the tram, in the park. Above the screen of the movie theater. Between the walls of the cafe. We can often see advertisements for mahjong clubs. (The sun is burning like fire. Gentlemen. How will you spend this humid and hot long day? Our house. It is as cool as late autumn. We have clean and delicate mahjong carved like ivory. We have kind and reluctant (courteous meaning) maids. Come on, gentlemen. Come and play cards. Playing cards is the most noble and interesting entertainment.

Every Sunday. Or after 5:00 on weekdays. Every club. Always crowded. When the lights are on, it is dazzling. Civil servants, businessmen, and students. They all like to play this game. It seems that they are tired all day long. If you don't come for four or eight rounds. It seems that the spirit cannot be restored. Every club. They almost all have several long-term fixed old customers. There is a manager of a large Wufudian (that is, silk and satin shop). After 3:00 pm every day. No matter how windy or rainy. The club must go. According to his secretary. Since February this year, his owner has not interrupted a day without touching cards. The famous writer Kikuchi Kuan. He is even more of a master in this field. When a card is touched in his hand. He can know whether it is Jiutiao or Batong without examining it. His technique. It is said to be a good story for a while. Many Japanese people praised and admired it very much.

Recently, the owners of bookstores have further fueled the flames and published many books on the study of mahjong. Such as Mahjong Entry. Mahjong Secrets. Scientific Mahjong Competition. Mahjong Yearbook. Mahjong Guide Mahjong Spring and Autumn, etc. It is really dazzling. There are many kinds. Small gambling. The Japanese also put in such research effort. Recently, the future. Their technology will definitely be better than blue.

The Japanese also play mahjong. I don't gamble on the outcome of money. It is completely a game nature. The club charges each guest who plays mahjong 60 cents for four rounds. The biggest loser pays 30 cents. The second loser pays 20 cents. The next loser pays 10 cents. The winner does not need to spend money. If there are not enough friends to meet the quorum. The club's maids can supplement. The club's maids. They have three tasks. One is to attract guests. The second is to supplement those who do not have enough card players. The third is the duty instructor for those who do not understand how to play cards. In every club. Hired these glamorous maids. Their playing garden. It will never be deserted. Because some customers. Although he does not have the hobby of Zhu (Bamboo Forest). But I can't resist the temptation of meat.

European Travel Correspondence (72)

— Liu Haisu

Touring the Palace of Versailles (7) Versailles

It was truly a bit heavy. A torrential rain and gale swept in. The entire sky was black. Seriously lacking even a sliver of light. The torrential rain soaked through our bodies, the dark clouds pressed down on our souls. This was truly a bit serious, for a very long time. The wind and rain still did not cease, as if they wanted to drag us into hell. I looked at the inky black sky, and I waited for what seemed like a long time. Finally, the wind and rain subsided. The black clouds also retreated a bit. A sliver of light penetrated through the green thicket. At the same time, a gust of cold air and a foul odor from myself also arrived. My skin and pores felt strangely uncomfortable. The birds in the forest also slowly began to chirp. So, we slightly poured out the accumulated water from the boat and continued to sit inside, rowing back. The head of the refined scholar was soaked by the rain, his permed hair hanging straight down his face, only touching his eyelids, brushing up and down. There were also many other tourists who had independently opened their boats and were floating in the middle of the stream. I ended up looking at their crazed faces.

"Although we have experienced hardships, we have also found it to be elegant and full of interest," said Mr. Chen Renhao leisurely.

Yes. The Palace of Versailles under clear skies is certainly not bad. But touring Versailles during a storm is even more of a point of pride for us, or perhaps even a masterpiece. Those who truly understand life, who want to thoroughly explore the depths of human interest, should seek interest in storms, in darkness, even in sin and ugliness. Because within these things there is a deeper poetry, a more profound and stimulating beauty. Ordinary people only find beauty in clear mountains and waters, only find goodness in doing things in a straightforward manner. These people have not truly understood life, nor have they tasted its profound meaning. The purpose of being a person is not to be a purely good and obedient son to one's father. Abundant food and clothing can never satisfy your ideals, but rather the pursuit of human interest in various deeper meanings. Therefore, the German music sage Beethoven liked to create music scores with the sounds of storms and gales, creating stirring, passionate, and tormented expressions. The French poet Baudelaire C. Bendelaie even described the facts of obscene sexual desire nakedly and without reservation, praising sin and evil. The modern great sculptor Rodin A. Rodin liked to praise the ugly. Many of his great works are seen by the common people as ugly and obscene things. We entered the Rodin Museum, and in the center of the middle room was a large work called (The Kiss). This is the pose of a naked man and woman embracing tightly. From all angles, there is not a single part of their flesh that is not trembling. This is also something that expresses sexual desire without reservation. There is also a sculpture displayed upstairs, titled (Ladelle Casquettiere). It is a naked old woman, resting her hands and looking down at her own body. Her skin is like chicken skin, her bones are thin, and she is very ugly. He wants to recognize a kind of decadent pleasure, or the sweetness of poison, in what is commonly considered ugly.

Gold Market Reaches New Heights

The price of gold suddenly takes a sharp turn upwards. Yesterday, the price of gold once again showed a sharp upward trend, transactions were active, and the market reached new heights. The upward trend continued, exceeding the 60 tael mark. However, there were fluctuations of two or three taels in both the morning and afternoon markets, with a total fluctuation of more than ten taels throughout the day. As for foreign exchange, it was generally stable, with a strong upward trend among dealers. Buyers were bold and fearless, with Fuchang, Xinyong, Xiangyuanxing, and others making large purchases. Yuanmaoyong and small retail investors were mainly selling. Although the morning market was long, it was still flat. As soon as buyers became active, the price immediately rose. The afternoon market was even stronger, with frequent increases of as much as seven taels. However, from morning to noon, there were ups and downs of three or four taels. Later, Zhifeng, Yongcui, Tai, and others showed unexpected buying interest, while Shunli, Yuanmaoyong, and others slightly sold off. Because the Indian exchange rate contracted, the market situation was even more sharp, and the price soared to 67-68 taels. However, the exchange rate happened to be on Wednesday, when there is usually no market. Afterwards, the price decreased slightly by two taels, settling at 66 taels. People could not help but feel apprehensive about the future.

Speculators rush to cover positions, pushing the price above 60 taels. The opening price for the October contract was 557 taels and 3 mace, a decrease of 9 mace. This was because the price of silver bars had increased by 16/3 of a cent, and the price of silver was the same as before. However, the gross price immediately turned higher, mainly because Fuchang, Yuancheng, Yongxinyong, Xiangyuan, and others were all buying, and the price of large bars was also increasing, so the price rose to 61 taels and 45 mace. After a slight decrease of one or two taels, the initial order was to hold the price steady, and then the price rose to 61 taels and 67 mace, then to 2 taels and 78 mace. Internally, the English Gold Bank mutually transacted September at 7 375/10000 pence, and November at 4375/10000 pence. Later, the price gradually declined by three or four taels, to around 61 taels. At 10:30 am, it broke into the 60 tael mark because Shunli, Wanxing, Taikangrun, and others all sold off, dragging the price down. At 10:45 am, the price was only 58 taels and 8 mace. Also, those who had previously shorted the market covered their positions, so after 11:00 am, the price once again rushed above the 60 tael mark, rising at a leisurely pace. The high point was five or six taels, with small fluctuations of one or two taels. At the close of the market, the price jumped to 65 taels. The afternoon closing price was 4 taels and 4 mace.

Afternoon closing price up 7 taels and 6 mace from the previous day. The afternoon market opened at 63 taels and 1 mace, then fell from 64 taels to 63 taels and 23 mace, due to selling by small retail investors. Afterwards, the Indian exchange rate fell by 4 annas, and the atmosphere suddenly became favorable. Rumors spread that India still wanted to sell silver, so dealers ignored the truth and rushed to buy, pushing the price to 67 taels and 8 mace at 3:00 pm. After 3:30 pm, the price jumped up another tael or so. At 4:00 pm, the price was around 7 taels. It returned to around five taels in a state of panic. Because the supply of goods from each route was more smooth than when the new goods arrived, and there was no hope for a revival in flour sales, it was feared that the market would have to loosen a little in accordance with the environment. As a result, the price for the current month was down 2 fen compared to the previous day, October was unchanged, November was down 1 fen, December was down 1 fen, and January and February were down 1 fen. Because the factory appetite was sluggish, the asking prices for middle and lower grades of wheat in the spot wheat market decreased by 1 or 2 fen, while the asking prices for high-quality goods remained stable. 500 bags of Jiangxi wheat were opened in the Kaisha market, but they have not yet been allocated to the factories.

Sugar Market: Daily Sugar Market Tends Firm

Yesterday's sugar market report from producing areas indicated that the spot price of Cuban sugar remained at 1.21875. New York futures sugar prices were 1.14 for September, 1.22 for December, 1.34 for March of next year, and 1.43 for May. Compared to the previous report, only September and March showed a slight decrease of one point each, with no increase or decrease in other months. The spot price of Javanese sugar was 8.875, with futures prices at 8.75 for September and 8.625 for October, also lacking significant fluctuations compared to the previous report. The new price for November was 8.50. In the market coordinated by the guild, the market for Dutch sugar No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar was calm, with very few transactions. High-quality white sugar in bags was priced at 8 taels, and finely ground white sugar reached 8 taels and 1 mace, with even quieter trading. Japanese sugar N mark was at 7 taels 9 mace, 1 mark at 8 taels 1 mace, TK mark at 7 taels 8 mace and a half, Minghua YT mark at 7 taels 8 mace and a half, YP mark at 8 taels, and TK mark at 7 taels 8 mace and a half, with relatively smooth trading. The market trend was firm. A transaction was reported by Jin Fa Hao, selling over a thousand bags of spot coarse granulated white sugar at 8 taels per bag, with a stable market. Hua Xin was reportedly selling off Dutch sugar, offering immediately loaded No. 20 medium granulated white sugar at a Dutch currency price of 5 yuan and 4 jiao and a half, new rules.

Silk and Tea: Jinhua's New Autumn Silkworms Will Soon Be Marketable

Silkworm Ants Have Been Doing Well... A Good Harvest Is Expected

The Jinhua old prefecture in Zhejiang Province generally produces silkworms earlier than other places. This year, due to the government's promotion and distribution of silkworm eggs, everyone is engaged in hatching and raising them, and the amount of feeding is not small. The silkworm ants have been doing well, and they have now started spinning cocoons on the mounting frames. The new cocoons can be removed from the frames within a few days, and a good harvest is expected.

Wuxi Autumn Silkworms: Early Broods Have Started Their Third Molt and Are Eating Leaves

Leaves are Priced at Three Yuan Per Load

The spring and summer silkworm harvests this year were disappointing, so farmers are paying special attention to this autumn silkworm crop, and most are raising more. However, due to the silkworm egg varieties, there is a big difference in timing. The early broods have already started their third molt and are eating leaves, while the later broods are only in their first molt. The silkworms are in very good condition, and a good harvest is predicted. Mulberry leaves are being sold for 2.5 to 3 yuan per load, but no one is selling them yet, because nine out of ten families are raising silkworms.

Lüzhuang Zhenmei Tea: Sales to England Show Slight Movement

Recently, the Zhenmei green tea from Lüzhuang, as well as from the Yingzhuang Jinlong, Tianxiang, Yihé, and Tongfu firms, has seen renewed activity due to orders from overseas. Transactions are not quiet, but the opening market prices remain low and weak. As for Qining black tea, since the Russian firms stopped purchasing, the Yingzhuang firms have seen no interest, and the market is completely stagnant.

Piece Goods: Eastern Goods Market Sentiment Wavering Upwards

Cotton Cloth Sales Are Slower Than Before

Recently, the market for cotton cloth from our factory has been quite stable, but sales are not as brisk as before. This is because the peak season is over, and the dyed cloth market has been hit hard since the Sichuan gangs stopped operations. Demand from the north is also slow. Fortunately, inventories are low, so there has been no downward trend. However, fine twill is rising without falling, and spot goods were even scarcer yesterday. All those who had stocked up in this street have sold out, creating a near-shortage situation, so hoarding is rampant. Guangdong and Shantou gangs are still searching for fine cloth, and the trend is weakening. However, the Jixiang Ren Zhong and Balloon brands are consistently out of stock, while coarse cloth is softer, with 14-pound and 13-pound "flying" styles showing only a slight decrease of about 5%. Coarse twill is increasingly quiet.

The rising trend of Eastern and Western piece goods was even stronger yesterday. Fine broadcloth, straight tribute satin, and straight tribute damask from the East were soaring, especially fine broadcloth, which was the most volatile. There was a difference of about 5% between the morning and afternoon markets, which is an unprecedented and strange increase. The real ball was sold for 3 mace in the afternoon, Huxinting for 2 mace 6.5 fen, Yan Muqiu for 2 mace 5 fen 7 li and a half, and Baizi for 2 mace 6 fen, all up by more than 1 fen compared to the previous day. Straight tribute satin First Grade was sold at 3 mace, Four Scholars at 2 mace 9 fen and a half, and straight tribute damask was up another 2.5 li, but there were no major changes in patterned goods. The "Release the Carp" and "Longevity" straight tribute damask from Saigon also rose sharply yesterday, selling at 2 mace 4 fen, while the rest remained firm.

Metals: Eastern White Iron Arrived Yesterday

Yesterday, 615 bundles (totaling 12,300 sheets) of Eastern white iron arrived at the Huishan warehouse, mostly seven-foot sheets. Exports have been lively recently, so various gangs in the Yangtze River and inland rivers have made some purchases. The Fuzhou gang emerged as a dark horse, purchasing a large quantity of 3,000 to 4,000 sheets yesterday. The price for 3' x 7' sheets was 1 tael 1 mace 2 fen and a half per sheet, and for 3' x 6' sheets, 9 mace 3 fen, reportedly up 1.5 fen compared to before. According to those familiar with this product, there is no scheduled arrival from Japan in the near future. If there are no arrivals within one or two weeks, the market outlook is bound to become more optimistic.

However, most sporting goods are imported, and the prices are expensive, making it difficult for those with limited means to purchase them. Several years ago, they witnessed the huge outflow of money in this area and immediately began to oversee the production of vests, basketballs, footballs, volleyballs, and other sporting goods based on their research. After several improvements, they have won a reputation for "exquisite and inexpensive." Major companies and stores across the country are happy to promote and sell them. It is said that the factory has many new products that are difficult to distinguish from foreign goods when placed together, and the wholesale price is only 50-60% of the foreign price. Foreigners are also happy to use them, so sales are booming, and they are shipping goods day and night. They are still worried about not being able to keep up and plan to find ways to expand the factory site, etc.

It is now said that this film has been scheduled to be released in the Central Grand Theater from the 6th, etc.

All preparations are currently underway, etc.

Changming Film Company announces that since the release of the first and second installments of The Burning of Pingyang City, the enthusiastic welcome from domestic and foreign audiences has opened a new record in the Chinese film industry that has never been seen before. Now, due to the requests of film distributors and audiences in various places, the third installment has begun shooting. However, in order to strive for perfection, we dare not be complacent. After a long period of consideration, hundreds of specially made costumes have been produced. The plot will integrate love, comedy, and martial arts in one furnace, with originality and not falling into old patterns. It is now being processed and rushed to be filmed, and it will be released soon. In order to reconcile the audience's tastes, a comedy blockbuster named (Two Great Heavenly Kings) is being filmed at the same time. The film has unique magic shooting methods, novel performances, and a sudden and funny plot. At present, the domestic film comedy item is the most lacking. The release of this film should refresh the audience, etc.

Paramount Pictures Company, Museum Road, announces that the film The Love Parade, published by the company, has been screened in several major theaters in the city for dozens of days, which is the longest record in the history of our country's film industry. Its box office success has been unprecedented even when it was released in Tianjin, Guangzhou, and Hong Kong. The value of this film is unmatched by any film company's products. The enthusiastic welcome of The Love Parade by people from all over the world is due to the effective direction of director King Liu Bieqian, who is glamorous but not lewd, satirical but not hurtful, and appreciated by both the refined and the vulgar, young and old. It is also due to the suitability of the male and female leads, Maurice Chevalier and Jeanette MacDonald, the thorough performance, and the clear singing, which are sufficient for people to watch once and again, again and again, and never tire of watching them. MacDonald's name has become a common phrase among general moviegoers. Now, Paramount Pictures Company has another fully colored musical dialogue film named The Smiling Lieutenant, also starring Jeanette MacDonald, with the male lead being Dennis King. MacDonald's expressions and singing have been praised by all those who have watched The Love Parade, and she has made even greater contributions in her new film. King is a famous stage actor in New York. He has rehearsed The Smiling Lieutenant on the American stage for more than a year before showing his appearance on the screen. Therefore, King starring in the film The Smiling Lieutenant is actually no different from re-enacting the stage play The Smiling Lieutenant. The scene in the film Colorful Flowers, which was previously shown at the Guanglu Theater and Dahua Open-Air Cinema in this city, in which a man sang a Russian love song on a colored background before going to the gallows, was taken from a section of The Smiling Lieutenant. The singer is King. The plot of The Smiling Lieutenant is based on the works of the 15th-century French poet François Villon. The short story writer McCarty used it to create a long narrative novel called If I Were King. Later, playwrights competed to use the novel's material to compile materials for stage dramas, and the opera world also arranged it into song plays several times, named The Vagabond King. Dennis King was one of the people who rehearsed it. Paramount Pictures Company re-adapted it into a film and hired the famous German director Lubitsch to direct it. Lubitsch has compiled and arranged fifty stage plays in Germany before joining the film industry. The musical film The Merry Widow is one of his directorial films. The music in the film was composed by three famous masters, William Bowstead, Berlin Hocker, and Rudolph Ming O, all of whom are outstanding figures in the world of cinema. In addition to the two important roles of Jeanette MacDonald and Dennis King, Warner Oland plays Duke de Polignac, the French Minister of War, Hugh Herbert plays King Louis XIV of France, Lillian Roth plays a street girl, and E. Alyn Warren plays the French King's comical barber. There are more than 2,000 other actors in the film. This film has now arrived in Shanghai and will be released after the autumn season, etc.

Youth Oasis

Awakened Youth

"Having knowledge is not about being old, lacking knowledge is wasting a hundred years." Now, I deeply believe this.

The day before yesterday, thanks to Wang's introduction, I was very fortunate to meet an admirable youth, a very young youth. Before I was introduced to him, I had already encountered his writings. At the time, I only admired his fluent writing and vivid style, his broad knowledge and thorough thinking. Of course, "Is it possible to read his writings without knowing the person?" But in reality, there are many places where it is not easy to achieve this goal, and it is also something that cannot be helped.

Now we have met him. He is a handsome young man, no more than seventeen years old, with a slender figure and a face full of innocence. He is lively, but he does not lose his composure. His amiable expression naturally makes him approachable, and he is also skilled in rhetoric. From his conversations, I know that he has read quite a few books. I had dreamed of seeing such a young man who could produce such sophisticated articles. How could I not be amazed and ashamed of my inferiority? I admire him twelvefold, and at the same time, I sincerely pray that the Chinese youth will all be as excellent as him and that everyone will be as enlightened as he is, and that they will be thoroughly enlightened in time.

The knowledge that modern youth should have and their mission are important topics in the third issue of "Shidai Qingnian" (Era Youth). The author, Ye Demao, is the young man I admired above.

It is an undeniable fact that modern youth are wandering on divergent paths. We only see and hear of the increasing number of fallen youth, emerging almost like bamboo shoots after the rain. If this continues, what will be the fate of the future new society and the Chinese nation?

"But when we study the reasons for their downfall, we find that most of them do not understand the background of the current era and the special environment and crisis of China. They are often assimilated by evil forces and blindly follow them. To remedy this situation, we must give them a clear understanding of the current era so that they do not blindly follow. At the same time, we must instill a sense of national consciousness, so that they know the crisis of the Chinese nation, prompting them to awaken and return to the battlefield of life as brave warriors, saving themselves, seeking a way out for the nation, and creating a blessing for the future society. Finally, we must make them understand the responsibilities and missions of youth."

Without reading the rest of his writing, we can deduce the layout of the whole article. The author has a clear mind and far-sighted vision. He uses a scientific approach to find the root cause of the illness and prescribes the right medicine to cure the modern youth's ailment. As such, it differs from ordinary articles that only talk about the symptoms of the illness without finding the root cause of the pathology, let alone offering any conclusions. It can be said that they do not even prescribe licorice or platycodon, and the result is nothing more than a torrent of scolding, cynicism, or shallow sympathy. The author, however, is completely different. Therefore, he divides his argument into several stages: 1. The Transformation of the Era; 2. Economic Aggression of the Powers in China; 3. The Crisis of China: A. The Collapse of the Rural Economy; B. The Emergence of the Exploitative Class; C. The Decline of National Consciousness; 4. Our Responsibilities and Missions.

The author's writing style is exceptionally fluent, like the Yangtze River, flowing a thousand miles without stopping. Therefore, it is impossible to copy and paste the first three sections. If we take some from the east and then reluctantly give up some from the west, it would be better to leave the readers to explore on their own, rather than leaving out details and harming the original spirit of the text. However, I dare to guarantee that you will not be disappointed, and you will even applaud and say, "How enjoyable and thorough!"

Now, I will only briefly introduce the fourth section.

Oh, youth! The era has already arrived, and we can no longer afford to hesitate and wander at the crossroads, or stand high in ivory towers. We can no longer afford to degenerate. We must rise up and strive to promote national movements, taking national consciousness as the central consciousness, and extinguishing all evil forces that are non-nationalist or lack a central consciousness. Because the only and greatest crisis in China today is the decline of national consciousness and the rise of anti-national consciousness! Oh, for the sake of saving ourselves, for the sake of the future of the nation, and for the sake of the survival of society, we must promote our national central consciousness movement. This is our only great responsibility and mission at present! However, we must also recognize that the national consciousness we advocate is not the simple national consciousness advocated by the Germanic or Yamato nations, which aims only to invade other nations for their own benefit. We want all the weak and small nations of the world to rise up and determine their own future. This is a necessary understanding before we take on our responsibilities and missions. In a nutshell, our responsibility is to save China from its current crisis, and our mission is to take national consciousness as the central consciousness to take on all responsibilities.

Finally, I must declare that my motivation for writing this article is not to promote someone like a celebrity. I ask the readers and the author to forgive me. My purposes are twofold: first, to introduce (Shidai Qingnian) to you. It may offer considerable guidance and comfort to generally frustrated youth. Second, to introduce the author of this article to you, so that you may learn from and be inspired by him. It is also a small tribute to the author. (Jiezhi)

Nanyang Model Middle School Adds Senior High School

Jiao Tong University Stops Sending Junior High Graduates

Pre-Collegiate Program to be Abolished

Nanyang Model Elementary School was originally reorganized from the affiliated elementary and middle schools of Nanyang University. Therefore, its teaching spirit is still consistent with that of Jiao Da. Every graduating class (junior high school graduates) can be promoted to Jiao Da's pre-collegiate program. After the Ministry of Education issued an order for all universities to abolish pre-collegiate programs, the Jiao Da authorities immediately followed the order and prepared to abolish the pre-collegiate program. It was decided that this year's pre-collegiate program would not enroll new students, but the graduates of Nanyang Model Elementary and Middle School this year could still be promoted to the pre-collegiate program according to the contract. After next year, they would no longer be able to be promoted in this way, so as to gradually abolish it. By 1933, this resolution could be completely abolished. After this resolution was made, the issue of Nanyang's school relocation arose immediately. Students and their families petitioned the Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Railways to allow them to continue operating without relocating. After receiving the petition, the Ministry of Education sent people to the school to investigate the situation and prepared a report, which was submitted to the ministry. The Ministry of Education believed that Nanyang was a private school, and Jiao Da was a national university. Private schools could not be promoted to national universities without an entrance examination. The Ministry of Education already had a clear order that even if the school had special circumstances and a contractual basis, it should not disregard the ministry's regulations. Therefore, it ordered the Municipal Education Bureau to order Nanyang not to guarantee the promotion of graduates, and at the same time, it directly informed Jiao Da not to accept them. As a result, the issue of Nanyang's promotion became a bubble. Despite all efforts, they could not succeed. Now, at the request of the students' families, the school has established a senior high school to prepare junior high school graduates for further education and to avoid the suffering of students dropping out of school. It is now ready, and most of the teachers are former teachers from Jiao Da's pre-collegiate program. For example, English is taught by Zhu Shuzheng, a former Jiao Da teacher, and mathematics is taught by Professor Zhang Lujing. All teaching methods are modeled after Jiao Da's pre-collegiate program to facilitate future entrance exams. This year, only one class of senior high school is being established, and no new students are being recruited. In the future, senior high school year two and three will be added gradually. After two years, the school can become a complete two-level middle school, etc.

Jiao Da Establishes College of Natural Sciences

Jiao Tong University previously received an order from the Ministry to add a College of Science to cultivate talents in materials testing and chemical analysis for various railway bureaus. After receiving the order, the school actively prepared. Initially, because the Nanyang school building was borrowed by Nanyang Model Elementary and Middle School, it repeatedly urged Nanyang to vacate the building in order to prepare for the site of the College of Science. Now, Nanyang cannot find a building for the time being, and Jiao Da's campus is large and does not lack a site. Therefore, it did not agree to return the building. Jiao Da could not wait for Nanyang to move out before starting the College of Science. Therefore, it was decided to establish the College of Science on the upper campus. The school already had very complete physical and chemical testing equipment. Therefore, there were not many difficulties in establishing the College of Science this time. However, because the railway bureau does not need many talents in physics and chemistry, the number of students is very small, only ten students per class. This year, the departments of Physics and Chemistry will be established first, and the departments of Mathematics and Geology will be added successively to complete the College of Science. Before the enrollment this year, the College of Science did not enroll students due to insufficient preparation for the previous enrollment. It is now scheduled to recruit ten new students at the Shanghai headquarters from September 7th to 10th. However, the school felt that the name "College of Science" was too common and changed it to the College of Natural Sciences, with the English name (Puro Science College). From now on, the school will have three independent colleges: Engineering, Railway Management, and Natural Sciences, with more than ten departments in total, which meets the requirements of the Ministry of Education's (University Regulations) and can be called a complete university. The enrollment time this time is late, and many people outside do not know the truth. In fact, the future career prospects of the students of this college are better than those of other colleges because the number of students is small and the demand is greater than the supply. It is said that the dean of the college is Xu Mingcai, the chairman of the Physics Department is Qiu Weiyu, and the chairman of the Chemistry Department is Ke Chengmao. Teachers will include Hu Dunfu, who will be hired, etc.

World Girl Scout Conference

— Junshan

The most surprising social phenomenon in modern society is the Boy Scout and Girl Scout movements. This movement is probably a very strong and promising form of communication in the international community today. When the Boy Scouts were first founded, they were greatly opposed by the generally conservative old gentlemen. When the Girl Scout movement developed, those old gentlemen were really speechless, thinking that they were born into the wrong world. But today, as far as we know, although the Boy Scout movement in the UK is well-developed, the Girl Scout movement is even more developed. The number of Girl Scouts in a country is even 100,000 more than the number of Boy Scouts.

This July, a World Girl Scout Conference was held at Foxlease Park in Hampshire, England. A total of 200 representatives from 30 countries attended. This was a very joyful and energetic gathering. Some of the representatives wore their national costumes and sang songs from various countries at the talent show. The conference decided that English, French, and German would be the official languages, but due to the prevalence of English, French and German were rarely used. Various issues of Girl Scouts were discussed at the conference, and the World Association of Girl Guides and Girl Scouts was also successfully established. Therefore, the results were very remarkable.

Sir Robert Baden-Powell, the founder of the Boy Scout and Girl Scout movements, also attended the conference. In his speech, he emphasized two points in particular: one is the value of the Girl Scout movement in the personality training of young people, and the other is the work that Girl Scouts can do in the international peace movement.

Tokyo Male and Female Youths Promote Abstinence from Alcohol

Commemorating the 8th Anniversary of the Great Earthquake

Tokyo News: Various public organizations of temperance and other groups in Tokyo, in order to commemorate the 8th anniversary of the Great Earthquake, launched a "No Alcohol Day" on September 1st, and held a lantern parade in Tokyo on the evening of August 30th, with 5,000 male youths and 500 female youths participating in the promotion of alcohol abstinence.

Returning Home—Patriotic "Two"

A. In terms of Moral Education: The quality of a school's ethos largely depends on its internal moral education, especially for girls' schools. The school's reputation is almost universally talked about. It goes without saying that Patriotic has a long history of thirty years and is trusted and admired by the general public. At the same time, the outside world has high hopes for it and is critical of it. In order to demand perfection, we sometimes heard criticism of Patriotic in the first half of the year, roughly saying that there were shortcomings in management and moral education. Indeed, it is no wonder that others discussed it, because the school's internal dormitories were insufficient, so many houses were rented in Tianbao Lane as off-campus dormitories. In fact, there were still resident teachers inside, which the outside world could not understand. Now, everything can be improved. According to Mr. Sun, the moral education strictly prevents being influenced by bad habits from the outside world. The current environment can indeed be lively and amiable in accordance with the regulations. I am not exaggerating, the daughters of Patriotic are indeed worthy of the name. Among the grade instructors and dormitory instructors who live on campus are Mr. Huang Shan, who is in charge of Boy Scout training, Mr. Shen Mingzhen, an expert in singing and dancing, Ms. Guan Suwen, a newly hired singing and dancing expert who graduated from Ginling Women's University, and Ms. Wei Xueqing, who is diligent and simple and very experienced in guiding students. There is also Ms. Chen Miaoming, who is proficient in English and piano, and Ms. Xu Junjing, who is rich in artistic talent. These ladies are all good teachers who are not easy to hire. With these ladies working together to promote moral education, they should not fail the high expectations of the outside world. In addition, with its beautiful location and beautiful gardens, it can be expected to create a new atmosphere. B. In terms of Academics: The level of each grade is greatly improved and the entrance examination is strict. There have also been slight changes in the academic aspects. Senior high school and year one have been changed to general subjects, and physical education has been changed to a three-year system. As for the teachers, it can be said that they have tried their best to recruit Ms. Nie Xiayu, a female elder who studied in the United States. Mr. Yu Jianhua is still the senior high school form teacher in year three, Mr. Li Tianxing is the form teacher in year two, and Mr. Sun Yimou is the form teacher in year one. The English teachers are still Mr. Su Zhaolong, Mr. Zhang Shian, and Mr. Hu Shangxin.

C. In terms of Facilities: The school site is appropriate and the various facilities are very suitable. The layout of the classrooms, desks, and chairs has been renovated, and the lighting is particularly sufficient. The library will be built with university library equipment, all of which will be purchased and retained. The gym is now under construction, located in Peach Garden. As for the beauty of the dormitories, it is rare to see in middle schools.

D. Patriotic has always had a history in literature and sports. I heard that the founder, Mr. Cai Zimin, and Principal Sun and Director Ji discussed and advocated using the power of literature to reform the thinking of general women and using educational methods to deeply serve society. They will convene a board of directors and educational experts to discuss specific measures in the near future.

Judging from this, it is not only gratifying for us married daughters to hear about it, but it is also good news for the future of women's education.

"Come and sit over there."

"Okay," I said, bidding farewell to Mr. Sun and walking towards Yu Shi's residence with him.

Oh, it's great. A purely Chinese-style single room, surrounded by trees, a yellow earth courtyard, a fence, and bean vines climbing on the fence, with purple flowers blooming. Outside the fence, there are many lush sunflowers, like a natural green screen. There are also a pair of spotless white geese and a pair of mallard ducks, adorning the unequal courtyard. Behind the house in the woods, there is also a clear stream, and looking over, you can see the "Hongkou Milk Shed" with many water buffalo. I said to Yu Shi, "This is just right for you. What a good painter." "Haha, I still have to learn to play the piano. I'll keep the stack to play to the cows."

This is the recent situation of our home. Our home has improved a lot, adding a lot of glory to us married daughters when we return to our husband's home. (Guangmei)
